1932.11.03

Expanding the Monthly Donation Campaign to Aid Northeastern Refugees Sincere 1

Recently, people from all walks of life in Shanghai, considering the arduous struggles of the righteous armies in the Northeast awaiting assistance and the urgent need for relief for the thirty million compatriots in the Northeast who are trapped in dire straits, have launched a monthly donation campaign. Its aim is to rescue the dying and heal the wounded. The declaration states: "If a person does not wish to do good, then so be it. But if one wishes to do good, then rescuing the dying and healing the wounded is the greatest act of benevolence. If a person does not wish to serve the country, then so be it. But if one wishes to save the country, then preventing its destruction and the loss of our homes is the ultimate way to serve the country." The words are deeply felt, and the tone is particularly passionate. We believe that if our countrymen have not yet forgotten the thirty million compatriots in the Northeast and the half of our nation's territory under the tyrannical rule of the Japanese, then they should respond to this monthly donation campaign promptly and join forces to help expand it.

Ever since the outbreak of the September 18th Incident last year, the Northeast has fallen under the violent grip of the Japanese. More than a year has passed since then, leading to the open staging of the puppet regime. Japan has also officially recognized the puppet regime, while our entire country is reveling in pleasure and luxury, just as before. It is like the merchants' daughters who do not know the sorrow of a fallen nation, like swallows nesting in curtains unaware of the danger. Only the righteous armies in the Northeast have spontaneously risen up to recover the lost territory, to fight for the dignity of our nation. They have consistently waged arduous and prolonged battles with the powerful enemy with unwavering perseverance. Their tragic blood has been shed across the broken land. Their loyalty and heroism are truly enough to move gods and spirits and shake the heavens and the earth. As for the thirty million compatriots in the Northeast, their homes were destroyed before the nation fell, and they were enslaved before the race was exterminated. They are struggling under the iron heel of the Japanese, writhing in agony, and have no way to appeal. Now, this year, the great flood in Harbin has caused a disaster, and the number of people displaced and wandering is also very large. The depth of their suffering and the urgency of their need for assistance are conceivable to us. The autumn grass beyond the Great Wall is bleak and the cold wind is harsh. These struggling righteous armies and refugees are now enduring hunger and cold, fighting desperately with the powerful enemy. We are eating and resting peacefully. If we were to disregard these righteous armies and refugees indifferently, like the people of Yue looking at the fat and lean of the people of Qin, without showing any sympathy, it would be fair to say that we have no heart or liver.

However, the reason why we are calling on the people of the country to strive to expand this movement is not primarily to persuade people to do good, nor to plead for the lives of the righteous armies and refugees in the Northeast, hoping to move the "compassion" of "benevolent people." We believe that this movement is a powerful test of the future of our nation's survival. If our nation can still maintain its spirit of national founding, if it has not yet forgotten this major trauma, if it is unwilling to let half of the Northeast's territory be lost in this way, then it should make extra efforts for this movement, and the lost territory in the Northeast will surely have a day of recovery. Our nation's life can certainly last for a long time. Conversely, if the people of the whole country indulge in pleasure and seek only temporary security, if they are unaware of the approaching death and unmoved by the impending disaster, then they will naturally look at this monthly donation campaign with indifference. The nation's vitality will completely disappear, which will prove it. And the darkness of our nation's future is as black as lacquer, and the danger is even more unimaginable.

Moreover, Japan's invasion of the Northeast has been carefully planned long before the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-1895. Under the conspiracy of its active continental policy, it will never be satisfied with seizing the Northeast. In other words, its iron hoofs will never stop at the Northeast. Hanzawa Gyokujo, the chief writer of the Japanese Diplomatic Times, wrote in an article on how Manchuria should be handled: "The last time I was in Fengtian, I said to Colonel Itagaki, a staff officer of the Kwantung Army, 'A child from my relatives' family also entered the Army Cadet School this year. After twenty or twenty-five years, he will also become Colonel Itagaki. For the development of future generations, please leave some work for them.' At first, Itagaki thought I was saying bad things about him. Later, when he understood what I meant, he said, 'What is this? The Manchurian problem is solved by us. Later, there will be the Siberian problem, the Pacific problem, and so on. Is there an end to the work of future generations?'" The implication is already self-evident. The Northeast Incident is like the eruption of a volcano. Once a volcano has erupted, it cannot be extinguished immediately. Therefore, our rescue of the righteous armies and refugees in the Northeast today is, on a large scale, to save our nation, and on a small scale, to save ourselves. The tyranny that the people of the Northeast are suffering today under the ambition of the violent Japanese can come upon our heads at any time. If we must wait until the country is destroyed and our homes are lost before we awaken, it will be too late, and regret will be of no avail.

We speculate that some people in the country may think that we are sincerely willing to make great efforts to rescue the righteous armies and refugees in the Northeast. However, today, our country's social economy is bankrupt, and livelihoods are becoming increasingly difficult. We are barely able to take care of ourselves, so how can we have the extra strength to make monthly donations? Their words seem to be true, but in reality, they are not. Today, Japan's rural areas are in decline, and the situation is also very serious. Rural debt has reached 700 million yen, with an average debt of 1,000 yen per household. After the September 18th Incident, Japanese farmers owed 80 million yen in taxes. The poverty of the people's livelihoods can also be imagined. However, since the Northeast Incident, the total amount of private donations for national defense supplies has been 6,282,630 yen. Even if they have no money to donate, they will give everything they have, even a chicken or a pig. If they, for aggression, and their people's donations are so enthusiastic, then we, for self-defense, for rescue, for national salvation, how can we not save on clothing and food, do everything in our power to help the righteous armies and rescue the refugees?

Countrymen, rise up, and strive to expand this monthly donation campaign to aid the righteous armies and refugees. The future of our nation is powerfully tested by this movement.

Important News

He Yingqin Orders Han and Liu to Withdraw Troops 2

And Telegrams Shen Honglie to Send Troops to Take Over Defense of Yantai and Longkou

(Nanjing) The Central Government has stipulated five measures to resolve the Jiaodong Incident. On the 2nd, Minister He of the Military and Political Department telegraphed Han Fuqu and Liu Zhennian to obey the order to withdraw troops, and also telegraphed Shen Honglie to take over the defense of Yantai and Longkou. The original texts of the two telegrams are as follows:

(A) Limited to immediate arrival, Commander-in-Chief Han of the Third Route Army in Jinan, Commander Liu of the Twenty-first Division in Yexian, Your Excellencies: In order to avoid conflicts between the two armies, three measures were stipulated on the 19th and telegraphed to you for your information. Subsequently, we received repeated telegrams from Chief of General Staff Jiang, stating that the Third Route Army requested an extension of the deadline for troop withdrawal due to transportation difficulties, and that a small number of troops should also be left in each county outside the temporary stationing area of the 20th Division to maintain law and order. After detailed verification of the above-mentioned sections, they are true. The following is specially restipulated: (1) The troops of the Third Route Army stationed in Jiaodong, except for one battalion of infantry stationed in each place to maintain the public security of Pingdu and Changyi counties, all other troops must be withdrawn to the original stationing area west of the Weihe River before November 8. (2) The 21st Division is temporarily stationed in the four counties of Fushan, Yexian, Laiyang, and Zhaoyuan, as well as Yantai and Longkou. (3) The defense of Yantai and Longkou is important. After the withdrawal of the Third Route Army and before the arrival of the troops of the 21st Division, Commander Shen of the Navy will send troops from nearby to maintain the public security of the area. (4) 700 members of the Ludong Militia will be stationed in Wendeng and Rongcheng, and 1,000 members of the Lunan Militia will be stationed in Muping to maintain public security in the area. (5) After the transfer of defense, military discipline should be rectified, and wait quietly for the central government to deal with it. For each of the above items, it is hoped that you will order your subordinates to earnestly comply with them and report them at any time. Military and Political Minister He Yingqin, Yinwu on the 2nd.

(B) Commander Shen of Qingdao, Brother Cheng Zhang, Your Excellency: Regarding the resolution of the conflict between the Han and Liu armies in Jiaodong, measures have been stipulated and telegraphed for compliance. We have just received a telegram from Chairman Jiang, stating that the defense of Yantai and Longkou is important, and that after the withdrawal of the Third Route Army and before the arrival of the troops of the Twenty-first Division, the Navy will send troops from nearby to maintain the public security of the area. It is found that the Third Route Army is limited to withdrawing before November 8, and the Military Commission will send Chief of General Staff Jiang Bocheng to the Third Route, Director Xiong Zhemin of the Administrative Office to the 21st Division Headquarters, and Secretary Gao Lingbai to Yantai and Longkou to supervise the withdrawal of troops separately. A special telegram is sent to you for your information, and it is hoped that you will send troops to take over the defense at that time, and we look forward to your reply. Military and Political Minister He Yingqin Winter, (2nd) Yinwu Print, (2nd Special Telegram)

(Jinan) After Jiang Bocheng received the Winter Telegram from He, when he notified Han Fuqu by telephone, He's telegram to Han also arrived. Han said that he would immediately issue an order to withdraw the defense. He Yingqin's telegram to Jiang Dong said: Limited to immediate arrival, Chief of General Staff Jiang Bocheng in Jinan, Brother Dong, Your Excellency, I have telegraphed and informed you. Since Brother Xiang has expressed his approval, the Jiaodong problem can be resolved satisfactorily before the League of Nations meeting. The international status of our country and the diplomatic benefits will be very great, and I am very happy and comforted. Brother Yingqin Donghai, (2nd Special Telegram)

(Jinan) Gao Lingbai is scheduled to return to Jinan from Qingdao tomorrow evening, and Xiong Bin will depart from Beijing for Jinan tomorrow. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) Han Fuqu replied to Foreign Minister Luo on the 2nd, saying, "I have received the telegram of the 30th. All that you said is for the glory of the country. It is hoped that the Jiaodong matter can be resolved peacefully. Please release your distant attention, and please convey my regards to Yan, Gu, Shi, and other gentlemen." (2nd Central News Agency Telegram)

(Jinan) At 8:00 a.m. on the 2nd, Han, together with Zhang Fang, Jiang Bocheng, Liu Yaoyang, and the directors of various departments, went to Chengnan Dai Dong Cave for sightseeing. Han told reporters that he had replied to Minister He, and everything was handled in accordance with the regulations in Minister He's telegram. As for the withdrawal of troops, it is necessary to wait until the Navy arrives to avoid interruption of defense. Up to now, no reply telegram has been received. (2nd Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Li Yuzhou and others, representatives of the people of Laiyang County, presented a memorial to the Central Government, requesting that after Liu Zhennian's troops are transferred elsewhere, no other troops should be sent to be stationed in order to avoid increasing the burden. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Qingdao) Li Qingshan, Commander of the Second Marine Corps stationed in Chengyang, received an order from Shen Honglie and led a team of more than 400 men to Qingdao on the evening of the 2nd, took the Zhaohe warship to Yantai to take over the defense. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Someone from a certain party received a telegram from Han saying that he had begun to withdraw in accordance with the order, and that the provincial army in Yantai and Longkou had decided to withdraw in sections in accordance with the various agreements, with the aim of completing the withdrawal completely before the 8th. It is said that Liu's troops will be transferred to Xuchang area in southern Henan, and the national government is consulting Ma Hongkui's opinion on the Jiaodong defense area. After all parties agree, an order will be issued for implementation. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Liu Suru, representative of Liu Zhennian, came to Beiping last night to visit Zhang, and returned to Tianjin this morning. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Liu Zhennian telegraphed Zhang, saying that he absolutely obeyed the peaceful handling and asked Han to withdraw his troops first, and his division would leave Shandong immediately. Any sacrifice is worth it. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Beiping) Xiong Xiling is going to Jinan tonight on official business. (2nd)

(Jinan) Song Zheyuan telegraphed Jiang Bocheng, saying, "I have just received a telegram from Xiang Fangdiyi Yanshu, and I am grateful for informing me that the Lu matter has been discussed by you and other measures have been agreed upon, which is indeed a way to solve it. I am very happy and comforted, and I hope that you will make every effort to promote it, not only for the sake of the people of Ludong. I have telegraphed back to Xiang Fang to urge its implementation. I know Guan Jin's attention, and I have telegraphed to inform you, Brother Song Zheyuan, Yin, on the 2nd." (2nd Special Telegram)

National Salvation Army Captures Taian Town 3

He Minhun's Troops Recover Chaoyang Temple

Righteous Army of 2,000 Attacks Phoenix County City and Station

(Qinhuangdao) The Northeast National Salvation Army, led by Commander-in-Chief Huang Yongping, joined forces with the troops of Pu Bingshan on the 2nd and captured Taian Town, capturing one Japanese tank and killing many Japanese soldiers. (2nd China United Press Telegram)

(Harbin) Today's Japanese newspapers reported that Taian Town, 30 miles west of Keshan, was captured. On October 20, 2,000 anti-Manchukuo troops appeared and besieged the city. The Japanese soldiers defended the city for ten days waiting for reinforcements. On the morning of the 30th, two teams of fresh Japanese troops came to reinforce, supplemented by airplanes, and attacked the righteous army north of Taian Town, forcing them to retreat. There were not many Japanese soldiers defending the city, and there were quite a few casualties. Captain Hayashi, the commander, was killed in battle, and 14 Japanese soldiers were killed and wounded respectively. The whereabouts of four employees of the South Manchurian Railway are unknown. It is rumored that Li Du, the leader of the anti-Manchukuo army in the Northeast, arrived in Boli on October 13. (1st Reuters Telegram)

He Minhun's Troops Capture Chaoyang Temple 4

(Shanhaiguan) He Minhun's Anti-Japanese Army in Rehe, Li Haifeng's Division, after joining forces with the troops of Meng Zhaoyan and Ma Zidan and others on the 30th and occupying Yixian County, captured Chaoyang Temple in the early morning of the 1st. A part of the Japanese army cut off the return route by destroying the Jin-Chao Road by Li's Division and retreated to the mountains of Chaoyang Temple. After being surrounded by Li, fierce fighting is still going on. (2nd China United Press Telegram)

(Shanhaiguan) Four Japanese planes of He Minhun's Anti-Japanese Army in Rehe, Wang Xingwu's Division, dropped bombs and bombed the army near Chaoyang Temple. After the army used rifles to shoot while lying on their backs, one plane crashed and the rest escaped. (2nd China United Press Telegram)

Wang Delin's Troops Fight Hard in Ning'an 5

(Dalian) Ha Xun, Wang Delin's National Salvation Army, with more than 6,000 men and many mortars, attacked Ning'an Ningguta at 2:00 a.m. on the 27th. The Japanese army, the 9th Division, and Ishida's troops responded to the battle, and airplanes were dispatched from Harbin to bomb. At 9:00 a.m. on the 28th, the artillery fire did not stop, and the stalemate lasted for more than 30 hours. The enemy has suffered many casualties, and Ning'an will be recaptured. (2nd China United Press Telegram)

(Shenyang) At zero o'clock this morning, about 2,000 members of the Big Sword Society were divided into two teams, one team attacked Phoenix County City, and the other team attacked Phoenix Station. Liu Cunhou and Others Jointly Mediate Sichuan Affairs 16

Pan Wenhua's Division Occupies Rongchang

(Hankou) Liu Cunhou, by order of the Central Government, united with Deng Xihou, Tian Songyao, Yang Sen, etc. to implement armed mediation. Liu Bangjun, commander of the troops, led two divisions to station in Sui'an, and Liu Bangjun himself went to Suining, and will telegraph to request the various armies to go to Sui to discuss a solution. The theory of the Suining Conference has thus been revived. If mediation fails, heavy troops will be united to intervene to avoid prolonging the war. To Liu Wenhui, he may only be forced to hand over power and retain a considerable position. It is now brewing. Jiang paid great attention to the Sichuan affair. When he went to Hunan, he summoned Xu Zhongqi, the Sichuan Provincial Party Committee, to inquire about the truth of the Sichuan situation, and asked him to draft opinions for selection when he returned to Han. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Hankou) After Jiangjin, Yongchuan, Dazu, and Hechuan were occupied by Liu Xiang, Liu Wenhui's first line of defense was lost. The war is still within Liu Wenhui's second line of defense. The war between Rongchang and Longchang gradually subsided at noon on the 31st. Liu Xiang once went to Yongchuan to supervise the army, and has now returned to Chongqing. Liu Wenhui is still stationed in Luzhou, and divides Luzhou, Xuyong, and Zi Nei into the third line of defense, arranges fortifications, and prepares for the final battle. (2nd Special Telegram)

The nearby militia and the garrison in the city were unable to suppress them due to their weak forces. There are also Red Army revolts in Juping Mountain in Xi County. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) Since the Allied Army captured Anyue in the Sichuan Provincial War, the war in northern Sichuan has come to an end. After that, the main battle will be moved to southern Sichuan, because Xuyong and other places in southern Sichuan are the source of Liu Wenhui's wealth, and he may not be willing to give up easily. According to the Sichuan Provincial Military Office, the commander-in-chief and the commander-in-chief of a certain route that the Allied Army previously intended to nominate have been completely cancelled in order to expand the scope of military affairs. However, for the sake of division of labor and cooperation, Shanghai is commanded by Tian and Deng, the central route is commanded by Yang Sen, and the downstream is commanded by Liu Xiang, and no other names will be established. (2nd Special Telegram)

Sichuan Members of the Central Committee Suggest Solutions to Sichuan Affairs 17

To be Discussed by Shi Qingyang at the Political Conference

Sichuan People Traveling in Beijing to Petition Today

(Nanjing) More than 50 Sichuan members of the Central Committee traveling in Shanghai, including Yang Shukan, Xiong Kewu, and Xie Chi, drafted solutions to the Sichuan affairs, first to narrow the scope of the war and shorten the time, and then to seek a fundamental solution. Xie Wuliang and Huang Shengxiang were specially sent to Beijing with an abridged version to be handed over to Shi Qingyang for discussion at the Central Political Conference on the 2nd and for reference by the Executive Yuan. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) Various Sichuan members of the Central Committee traveling in Shanghai suggested to the Central Government the following solutions to the Sichuan affairs: 1. Follow the principles of governing Sichuan promulgated by the National Government in the 17th year of the Republic, and order the Sichuan generals to comply with them, and stop the war immediately. 2. In accordance with the resolution of the Second Plenary Session of the Central Committee, send Sichuan members of the Central Committee with a high reputation to Sichuan to supervise and guide the generals to comply with them. 3. In accordance with the resolution of the Second Plenary Session of the Central Committee, reorganize the provincial government and improve its organization. 4. Abolish the bad system of defense zones, obey the Central Government, and return the people's wealth and various administrations to the provincial government. 5. Organize a Disarmament Committee, with ten divisions as the maximum limit, and station them in western Sichuan, Ningyuan, Leima, Ping, Songli and other places to strengthen the border defense. The expenses for disarmament and reorganization shall be borne by the Central Government and the provincial government. 6. Implement independent military supplies, and the Central Government shall send personnel to be responsible for presiding over them. 7. Implement a militia system, and refer to the military industry policy, so that the demobilized soldiers and the militia can be used for defense in case of emergency, and engage in production in peacetime. 8. Thoroughly reorganize finance, and all exorbitant taxes, miscellaneous taxes, debt pads, and advance levies should be considered and abolished as soon as possible to reduce the suffering of the people. 9. For the border defense and bandit suppression troops, please order Liu Wenhui and Liu Xiang not to mobilize a single soldier or soldier for internal wars. 10. Regard whether each army can obey the orders of the Central Government as the standard of obedience or rebellion. If there are those who are willing to make trouble, please the Central Government suppress them by force. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The special committee for stopping the Sichuan war organized by the Sichuan Fellowship Association in Beijing has decided to petition the Central National Government Executive Yuan on the 3rd to actively stop the Sichuan war and seek a fundamental solution. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) Shi Qingyang, Chairman of the Mongolian Committee, plans to invite fellow Sichuanese traveling in Beijing in his private capacity within a few days, together with Zeng Qiangqing, Chen Peiquan, and Chen Yunge, to discuss ways for Sichuan people to unite, so as to contribute opinions on the Sichuan issue at any time. Zhang Qun took a boat to Han on the morning of the 2nd to visit Jiang to discuss ways to stop the Sichuan war. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) Dai Jitao said that he advocated taking the order of the National Government in the 17th year of the Republic as the principle for solving the Sichuan affair, and then combining the opinions of all parties to draft a detailed speech, which has been passed by the Central Political Conference and handed over to the Executive Yuan for handling. The Yuan will draft the implementation steps in a few days, ordering the generals in Sichuan to earnestly comply with them. (2nd Special Telegram)

We then occupied the old nest of Ge Yuan, destroying more than ten fake military factories and other organs. (2nd Special Telegram)

(Nanchang) Chiang Kai-shek believes that various units have deep-rooted concepts of their own territory, which leads to bandits being suppressed in one place and fleeing to another. (Nanchang) The Jiangxi bandits, due to our strict search and suppression, find it difficult for small groups to survive and are consolidating into larger units. For example, those attacking Zaojia City are said to be the Fifth Division, but in reality, they only have a thousand or so rifles. Recently, when the bandits are defeated, they often abandon their rifles and flee, unlike before when three or four people shared one rifle and would not retreat even in death. The bandits captured by the Eighteenth Army all have hair several inches long and are covered in dirt, which shows their suffering. Zhu De and Mao Zedong's main forces have all fled east to northern Fujian. (2nd Special Telegram)

Central Political Conference 21

Decides on Two-Step Approach to Sichuan Issue

(Nanjing) The Central Political Conference held its 330th meeting on the morning of the 2nd, chaired by Ju Zheng. The following important cases were resolved: (1) Regarding the Sichuan dispute, it was decided to reiterate the National Government's order attached to November 7th of the 17th year and hand it over to the Executive Yuan to detail the implementation measures, formulate a plan, and report it to this conference. (2) Approved the Shanghai Municipal Government to issue a six million yuan bond for the restoration of the municipality, using the city's wharf donation income as a fund for principal and interest repayment, and handed it over to the Legislative Yuan. (3) The Financial, Economic, and Legal Systems Groups reported on the review of the Legislative Yuan's request to order the Ministry of Finance to draft the Bank Convertible Note Issuance Law and the Central Bank Law. It was believed that this case should be handed over to the Executive Yuan for detailed study to formulate gradual unification of convertible notes and development of the Central Bank methods, and then review them. It was resolved to pass the review opinions. (2nd Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) The Central Political Council held a meeting on the morning of the 2nd. The important cases are as follows: (1) The Sichuan issue was decided on a two-step approach: (A) Order the Executive Yuan to reissue the National Government's order of November 7th of the 17th year. (B) Order the Executive Yuan to formulate detailed implementation rules based on the principles of the previous order, jointly study and decide with Central Committee members familiar with the Sichuan situation, and then report to this meeting for discussion. (2) The regulations for issuing six million Shanghai Municipal Restoration Bonds and the principal and interest repayment schedule were resolved to be submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review. (2nd Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) According to the Executive Yuan's submission from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the telegram from Representative Yan, who attended the League of Nations meeting, the General Rules for Resolving International Disputes in 1928 and the Convention on Improving Methods of Preventing War in 1931 are valued by governments of various countries. Should our country formally join or declare preparedness to join during this conference? The Executive Yuan submitted it to the Central Political Council for discussion on the 2nd. It was decided in principle that it could be joined and submitted to the Legislative Yuan for review. (2nd Special Telegram)

Japanese Technicians Inspect Jilin Province Forests 22

(Shenyang) Technician Nakamura from the Colonization Ministry, Technician Iwa from the Shenyang branch of the Colonization Ministry, Technician Aoyama from Manchukuo, and four entrusted individuals from the Special Affairs Department, starting from the 28th of last month, conducted an aerial survey of the large forests of Jilin Province. At 2 p.m. yesterday afternoon, they flew back to Shenyang by plane. Technician Iwa immediately began drafting a report to be submitted to the province. The group flew from the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway to the Jidun Railway along the Motianling, Laowengling, and Changbai Mountain areas, spending five days and covering a distance of 10,000 meters for detailed investigation. The investigation was just completed. Although they were unwilling to disclose the results of the investigation, such as the quantity and quality, they all said that the abundance of forests in Jilin Province is indeed a great source of wealth for Manchuria and praised it unreservedly. (1st Electric Communication Agency Telegram)

Results of Yellow River Inspection 24

Zhang Hanying's Talk

After the inspection, he will go to Hankou to meet with Chiang Kai-shek and report. This is because Chiang Kai-shek said that as long as there is a way to control the Yellow River, funds can be raised. The results of this inspection show that controlling the Yellow River is not impossible. The most important things are (1) dredging the mouth of the sea, (2) narrowing the river channel in Henan province, and (3) digging the Wushu Mountain to prevent the Tao River from flowing north into the Yellow River and south into the Wei River. Important Foreign Telegrams

No Matter the Change of the Next President, US Policy Toward the Far East Will Not Change 60

Maintain the Open Door Policy and Preserve the Territorial Integrity of China

Naval Policy Will Shift with the Progress of the Sino-Japanese Case

National News Agency, Washington, 1st: With the primary election period for the US presidential election only a week away, according to responsible sources here, regardless of the outcome of the primary election, the US policy toward the Far East seems likely to remain unchanged. Whether the next government belongs to the Republican or Democratic Party, it is expected to adhere to the traditional Pacific policy, namely the sanctity of treaties, the open door for trade, and the territorial integrity of China. Moreover, the current US policy toward Manchuria is a strictly government policy and has never involved party views. Therefore, during the previous session of Congress, influential senators and representatives of both the Republican and Democratic parties did not severely criticize it. Even among the public, it is expected to be generally approved by public opinion. However, the effectiveness of the current policy is entirely dependent on public opinion. Some people here believe that if the government changes, the public's reaction to the Manchurian situation may be expressed in new ways. This is because President Hoover and Senator Borah, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, both obstructed the public's inclination to boycott Japanese goods. It is not known whether a new sentiment of non-official boycott of Japanese goods will re-emerge among the people once the person in charge of diplomacy changes. As for trade, the change of government will naturally bring new hopes for increasing Pacific trade. However, tariff revisions will have little impact on the entire Far East trade, because the United States does not tax many important products from the Far East. Even for agricultural products, if the Democratic Party revises tariffs, it will not raise them. Both the Republican and Democratic parties are eager to support silver prices and find ways to raise them in order to benefit the ten western silver-producing states in the United States. However, although China is on a silver standard, according to experts here, the Chinese only hope for the stability of the remaining price. As for military spending, regardless of whether the Republican or Democratic Party is in power, they are expected to continue to work to limit armaments. However, in the coming years, the United States may be seen carefully discussing its naval policy. However, this matter must shift with the results of the arms reduction conference and the future progress of the Manchurian dispute. As for island policies, the two parties have very different opinions, which will have repercussions on Far East relations. The Democratic Party platform advocates the independence of the Philippines, while the Republican Party platform does not mention it. The Republican Party platform states that the method of governing Hawaii remains as before. Although the Democratic Party platform does not explicitly state it, William, the leader of the party, proposed a case when he was chairman of the House Territorial Committee in the previous Congress, advocating major reforms in the legislative system of Hawaii and suppressing the power of Japanese residents.

Reuters, Washington, 1st: The US presidential election campaign is now intensifying. Hoover and Roosevelt are campaigning everywhere, hoping to influence the views of voters. However, according to various signs, Roosevelt seems to have a better chance of winning. In betting on the election results, Roosevelt has a three-to-one advantage. However, the Republican Party remains confident that Hoover can be re-elected as president. Personally, Hoover, as the incumbent president, can slightly gain an advantage. However, Roosevelt's demeanor is also enough to make voters admire him. Roosevelt is a relative of the late President Roosevelt. Politically, there are no significant differences between the policies of the two parties. They have similar views on import tariffs, except that the Democratic Party attacks the current tariffs as too high. The people of the United States suffer, and the financial difficulties are all attributed to President Hoover. Whether this accusation is appropriate or not, it is enough to make voters lean to the other side and give them the opportunity to clarify the situation.

Japan Urgently Prepares for War 62

Factories Rush to Manufacture Military Explosives

Osaka Dispatch from the China United News Agency: Since explosives are the most important supplies for future wars, we will briefly record how the Japanese imperialists are expanding their gunpowder factories. The Japanese Army Ministry has built ten gunpowder factory branches near Tadaumi in Hiroshima Prefecture. The necessary machinery has been formally contracted with the Japan Foundry Company. At the same time, the Iwahana, Oji, and Ryokuyo gunpowder factories also plan to increase the number of poly-star nitric acid suction machines, and are also trading with the Japan Foundry Company. In the naval field, in order to meet the demand for eight hundred explosives, a temporary contract has been established with the Imperial Explosives Company. As a result, the Imperial Explosives Company is extremely busy, renovating the strong guncotton nitration, smokeless gunpowder drying and airing, solvent recovery, and other major factories. Because the Navy Ministry forcibly ordered the urgent production of military chemicals, the Maizuru Explosives Department ordered work day and night, causing an explosion due to overheating of sulfuric acid raw materials, killing and injuring seventeen workers on the spot. Not long ago, a private factory also used five million yuan of Yazaku Hydroelectric Power Company funds to establish a nitric acid plant in Nagoya Atsuta. The Fukushima Genta factories in fertile Japan have also received secret orders from the military to manufacture poison gas and perchloric ammonia chemicals. Other projects such as the aerial nitrogen fixation project (ammonium sulfate factory) are also increasing production and improving explosive products. The above examples clearly show how urgent the second imperialist war is.

World Economic Conference 69

The Preparatory Committee Discusses the Gold Standard

France, the United States, and Belgium Oppose the British Plan

Reuters, Geneva, 1st: The experts of the preparatory committee of the World Economic Conference gathered here this morning to discuss the gold standard. British representative Philip spoke the most, saying that the rise in prices and the removal of trade barriers are two necessary prerequisites for currency equalization. Mr. Fei also read a section of the Ottawa Agreement to explain the British plan, but the British representative's views were strongly opposed by the representatives of France, Belgium, and the United States. They all believed that Britain's abandonment of the full gold standard forced neighboring countries to increase their tariff barriers.

Havas, Geneva, 1st: When the Economic Subcommittee of the Preparatory Committee of the World Economic Conference met, French representative Subei declared that there were three policies that France could choose from: raising tariffs, abolishing promises on international contracts (i.e., commercial treaties), and opening the border to allow its own producers to be trapped. However, France ultimately adopted the method of quantity restriction, because in terms of France and those who trade with France, we believe that the harm of this method is the lightest.

Japanese Goods Are Dumped in British Territories 74

The British Parliament Discusses Boycott Methods

British Trade with Russia Continues to be Maintained

Reuters, London, 1st: In the Lower House tonight, a Conservative MP showed samples of Japanese white silk and colored silk, saying that Japanese goods were being dumped in British territories. Stricter measures should be taken than those stipulated in the Ottawa Agreement to stop the dumping of Japanese silk. The reasons are as follows: (1) Japanese workers work 60 hours a week and only get 7 shillings and 3 pence in wages, while the UK has to pay 35 shillings for 48 hours a week. (2) The Japanese government guarantees bad debts. (3) The Japanese imitate English goods. The silk he showed is sold for only 30 to 35 shillings per yard, while the same English silk costs 56 shillings per yard and has no profit. English factories producing this silk are gradually closing down. If the government does not remedy it quickly, this industry will soon disappear.

Reuters, London, 1st: The two Houses of Parliament debated the issue of trade with Russia this evening. Some people in the Upper House proposed that trade with Russia should not be resumed until Russia repays its debts. Government representatives opposed this proposal, saying that British trade with Russia has increased from 2 million pounds in 1928 to 7 million pounds last year. If this trade is stopped, it will increase unemployment in the UK and will not make Russia pay its debts. This proposal was later withdrawn.

British Unemployed People Again Riot in London 75

Police Exert All Efforts to Suppress the Riot

National News Agency, London, 1st: Representatives of the unemployed people outside the British capital wanted to petition the Lower House of Parliament to abolish the livelihood investigation system (i.e., asset measurement), which led to disturbances in a large area of London today. Thousands of unemployed people in the capital suddenly gathered and demonstrated. The police initially failed to cope with the situation, and then tried to separate the demonstrators into more than a dozen sections and suppress them separately. When the demonstrators' momentum gradually weakened, they surrounded them again, and finally restored order in two hours. The representatives of the unemployed people outside the capital tried to separate themselves from the demonstrators from beginning to end. They told people afterwards that they would continue to adopt a policy of passive resistance and carry out orderly demonstrations and publicity, so as to express their grievances to the authorities and achieve the purpose of petitioning. According to reports, today's demonstration was held in Westminster. Representatives from outside the capital and unemployed people in the capital filled the streets. The more people gathered, the more crowded it became. The police saw that it would be difficult to control the situation, so they began to expel them. As a result, small conflicts occurred in Whitehall, Strand, and Trafalgar Square. Many shop windows were destroyed. On the Victoria Embankment, the public destroyed streetcars and overturned cars. Mounted police and foot police repeatedly suppressed them, and expelled them until about 11:00 in the evening. Except for a few places where there were still small conflicts, the city was generally back to normal. More than 20 demonstrators were arrested, and many people were slightly injured. Several policemen were also hit by stones, but no one on either side was seriously injured. During the disturbance, the police always prevented the public from reaching the Parliament.

Twenty-One Banks in Nevada, USA, Suspend Business 78

The Market Is Weak and Financial Turnover Is Unstable

The Governor Borrows Money from Washington for Relief

National News Agency, Reno, 1st: Nevada, USA, announced today that it will temporarily suspend payments in the state for two weeks. Twenty-one of the twenty-five state banks have been ordered to suspend business. In a subsequent announcement, they will be temporarily managed by State Bank Auditor Wenfield. (According to the United States, there are national banks, state banks, and city banks, depending on the scope of their business.) Currently, Governor Barchai is in Washington, hoping to borrow a large sum of money from the Financial Relief Department to relieve the financial community in the state. According to the recent cause of this financial trend, due to the fall in livestock prices, the consumption of meat in the summer months has been reduced, and the price has plummeted. Although consumption has increased recently, the price of meat has not increased. As a result, the money borrowed by various livestock industries from banks has become bad debts, and the financial community feels that the turnover is not working. Now that the Governor has gone to Washington and the Deputy Governor Griswold has announced the temporary suspension of payments, the financial situation has become even worse. All banks that have not suspended business have followed the temporary suspension of payments regulations, restricting business, only handling check accounts and daily business, neither lending nor forcibly unwinding. The financial community has lost its turnover effectiveness. Nevada's resources are mainly based on mining, animal husbandry, tourism, and divorce cases. Now that the price of silver has plummeted, the number of tourists and divorce cases has also decreased sharply. Coupled with the stagnation of the animal husbandry industry, one of the states with the greatest civil wealth in the United States has also suffered this major blow. The state has a population of less than 92,000, and the average wealth per person is 6,318 yuan.

A Great-Grandson Cut Off an Old Grandmother's Life 79

The Old Customs of Yugoslavia Should Be Reformed

Havas, Yugoslav Capital, 1st: In Yugoslavia, a house collapsed some time ago, and an old man, 113 years old, was rescued from the rubble and was safe and sound, which was spread as a topic of conversation. Today, an old woman, 124 years old, died, which shows that the spirit of heaven and earth is concentrated in the southern country. Otherwise, how can there be so many people who live to be 100 years old? The old woman's death is worth recording. The old woman was old and weak, and her limbs lost their function. One day, she lay on the head of the bed, and her family suspected that she was dead, so they prepared her for burial. According to the old customs of the place, the youngest member of the family should pierce the abdomen of the deceased with an iron bolt before the burial. Although this custom has been repeatedly prohibited by the authorities, the general public has disobeyed it. After the old woman was buried, her young great-grandson performed the ancient ritual according to the rules. Unexpectedly, the iron bolt hit her abdomen, and the old woman woke up in extreme pain. Afterwards, she died soon due to her old age and weakness and could not bear the pain.

The Shandong Issue is Completely Resolved 81

The Korean Army will Withdraw First, and then the Liu Army will Leave Shandong

Gao Lingbai Went to Yantai to Monitor the Actions of the Two Armies

Qingdao Correspondence: Since the conflict between the Korean and Liu armies in Jiaodong, they have been in a stalemate for more than a month, and have not yet been resolved. The Liu army in Yixian City has repeatedly tried to break through and escape due to lack of food, but has been repelled by the Korean army, and its strength has been greatly reduced. Recently, Liu Zhennian himself, who was trapped in the city, is not as stubborn as before, and expressed his willingness to obey the orders of the Central Government. The Liu's troops in Laiyang City also broke out of the city and fled south on the 27th due to lack of goods. When they reached Changzhi Town in the territory of Jimo County, they were quickly detected by Rong Guangxing, the commander of the 87th Brigade of the Korean Army. He immediately telegraphed the Third Route Army Headquarters to ask for a team to intercept them, and ordered his subordinates to be on strict alert to prevent them from fleeing south. The Qinghai garrison, fearing that the defeated soldiers would flee into the city and hinder the security of the city, also urgently dispatched 400 marines to Jimo to deploy. Cooperate in blocking. The next day (28th), the Jin Dianbang Regiment of the 87th Brigade stationed in Gaomi Jiaoxian was ordered to attack. It immediately united with the local militia to surround Changzhi Town. The Liu army resisted slightly, and then raised a white flag, willing to hand over their weapons. It is estimated that more than 300 rifles and more than 30 submachine guns were seized. All captured officers and soldiers were ordered to be given severance pay. It is said that the actual number of Liu's troops in Yixian and Laiyang, in addition to the dead, wounded, and captured, is currently about 14,500. Since Liu Zhennian has expressed his willingness to obey the orders of the Central Government, this matter is easy to handle. Recently, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek sent Zhuang Bocheng, Zhang Fang, and others to Jinan to discuss the mediation method with Han Fuju. Han has fully agreed to withdraw his troops first. Chiang Bocheng is in Jinan and is responsible for the Korean side. Gao Lingbai went to Yantai, and Xiong Bin went to Yixian, and was responsible for the Liu side. Mr. Gao took the Jiaoji Road train last night and arrived in Qingdao at 7:30 this morning (31st). Mayor Shen Honglie personally went to the station to welcome him. Currently, Mr. Gao is staying at the Xinmin Hotel. I went to visit Mr. Gao and visited Shen Honglie at the Municipal Government to inquire about the withdrawal of troops from the Korean and Liu armies. Henan Province Requests the Establishment of a National Museum 83

Kaifeng Dispatch: The Henan Provincial Government, considering that Henan Province is located in the Central Plains and is the birthplace of Chinese culture, and that in recent years, through the efforts of the Academia Sinica and the Provincial Government, many ancient artifacts have been unearthed, all of which are valuable cultural relics, believes that a national museum should be established in Bian (Kaifeng) to store these unearthed artifacts, and to collect and display flora, fauna, and minerals from across the country for academic reference. A formal petition has been submitted to the Executive Yuan, requesting approval for its establishment. The original petition is as follows: "We respectfully note that the rise and fall of a nation depend on the flourishing and decline of its culture. In order to promote public education and propagate culture, all countries have established museums to supplement the shortcomings of school education and social education. The function of a museum is not only to preserve ancient artifacts and documents, but also to systematically introduce ancient culture, modern natural specimens, and models to the general public, to cultivate their love for the culture of their motherland and their interest and ability to strive for modern civilization. Therefore, museums have a significant impact on social education. The Ministry of Education previously stipulated in its social education program that the government should establish a central museum in the capital and select several important cities to build museums with state funds. This intention is far-sighted and admirable. Henan Province is located in the Central Plains and is the birthplace of Chinese culture. In recent years, many ancient artifacts have been unearthed, which are of great importance. It is indeed necessary to establish a complete museum. We respectfully submit the detailed reasons to your esteemed Yuan: (1) Historical Aspect: China is one of the earliest countries with a culture in the world, and Henan Province is the birthplace of Chinese culture. Since before the Zhao and Song dynasties, all dynasties have established their capitals here. After thousands of years of history, famous places, historical sites, steles, stone carvings, and other ancient relics are found everywhere underground. These items can all be used for the textual research of ancient culture. For example, the oracle bone inscriptions discovered in Anyang in recent years are sufficient to determine the civilization of the Yin and Shang dynasties; the ritual vessels from Xinzheng are sufficient to determine the rites and institutions of the Eastern Zhou dynasty; the statues from Luoyang and Gongyi are sufficient to determine the art of Buddhism during the Northern Wei, Qi, and Tang dynasties; and the pottery from Mianchi is sufficient to determine the social conditions of the Stone Age. These are just the most prominent examples. In other places such as Ji, Hui, Hua, Jun, Xia, Mi, Dengfeng, Yanshi, Mengjin, Nanyang, Tongbai, Xinyang, Xiangcheng, Yanling, and Xihua, ancient artifacts are often discovered. However, due to the lack of well-equipped institutions for preservation and collection, they are often colluded with by a small number of unscrupulous elements who buy them up and take them away, resulting in the loss of treasures left by our ancestors for thousands of years. This is truly regrettable. In view of this, the Provincial Government, in conjunction with the Academia Sinica, established the Henan Antiquities Research Association in the 20th year (of the Republic), which is specifically responsible for the investigation, excavation, and research of ancient artifacts. However, the preservation of ancient artifacts is the responsibility of the Henan Museum, which is small in scale and insufficient for development. This is the first reason for establishing a museum to preserve ancient documents. (2) Geographical Aspect: Henan is located in the Central Plains, directly accessible to the north, south, east, and west via the Longhai and Pinghan railways. Transportation is extremely convenient. Recently, the call for the development of the Northwest has spread throughout the country. If we want to realize the development plan, the first step is to collect and display various products of the Northwest as much as possible, and introduce them to the general public, to arouse their determination to participate in this development work. The only institution that can fulfill this responsibility is the museum. Henan is the first gateway to the Northwest. If Henan has a complete museum, those who are concerned about the Northwest do not need to go to the Northwest in person. They only need to set foot in Henan to understand everything about the Northwest. In his book "Travels of Marco Polo," Marco Polo described the Eastern culture in great detail. Europeans who read it were filled with admiration, which eventually led to the discovery of the Eastern sea route. The descriptions in travelogues are only indirect impressions, but their function is sufficient to promote the successful integration of Chinese and Western cultures. The museum is a direct promotion of facts. When we enter it, our perceptions are subconsciously changed. Its impact is far beyond what travelogues can compare. This is the second reason for establishing a museum to realize the development plan of the Northwest. (3) Production Aspect: Henan is located in the Huai and Yellow River basins, with fertile soil and abundant resources. Due to climate and geographical conditions, all natural products such as flora, fauna, and minerals have a tendency to connect the north and the south. This point is extremely important in natural science and should not be ignored. In recent years, biological research institutes and geological survey institutes have been established in various parts of the north and south. Although Henan also has plans to establish such institutions, the former has only recently been planned and organized by Henan University, and is limited to Baiquan. The latter is also small in scale and insufficient to shoulder this important task. According to the field investigations of general scholars in recent times, new species of fish are often found in Henan that are different from common species. This is truly a major discovery in academia. It is urgent to collect them extensively for comparative research. This is the third reason for establishing a museum to connect the changing relationships of natural products in the north and south. (4) Political Aspect: Finally, from a political perspective, since the establishment of Luoyang as the capital, Henan has become an important town in our country. The number of Chinese and foreigners traveling back and forth has increased many times. The western section of the Longhai Railway is progressing rapidly, and its hub is of great importance. It seems appropriate to strive for perfection in cultural facilities, to give a fresh impression to both Chinese and foreigners. This is the fourth reason for establishing a museum to promote the country. In summary, a complete national museum is urgently needed and has great benefits. If we do not quickly plan to establish one, it will be insufficient to meet the needs of the times. We propose to establish a national museum in the open space near Longting in Kaifeng City, in accordance with the provisions of Item 3, Section 1, Article 5 of the Education Program, to collect flora, fauna, and minerals from across the country, as well as valuable cultural relics, and display them extensively to achieve perfection. The various unearthed items obtained by the Anyang Yin Ruins Excavation Team of the Academia Sinica can be directly stored in the museum after the research is completed and returned to the province, so as to avoid disputes. In the future, all unearthed ancient artifacts in various counties should also be collected extensively and displayed together, so that the cultural relics left by thousands of years can be permanently preserved in Henan, the birthplace of culture. When people of insight from all over the country come to visit and study, they will surely be inspired and excited, and will think of ways to promote and expand them, which will be of great benefit. As for the establishment funds, in accordance with Item 1, Section 1, Article 5 of the Education Program, the construction and operating expenses of museums in important cities should be allocated by the government. In addition, the provisions of Items 6 and 7 of the same article, which stipulate that "the construction and equipment costs of museums in various provinces shall be set at 500,000 yuan," and "the operating expenses of museums in various provinces shall not be less than 50,000 yuan," are proposed to be allocated from the Geng款 (Boxer Indemnity Funds) for application."

Profound Writings of Westerners After Investigating the Northeast 84

Civil Servants and Elementary School Teachers All Hold Anti-Japanese Sentiments

The Puppet State Army Especially Unwilling to Fight Against the Righteous Volunteer Army

Since the September 18th Incident, various countries have paid close attention to the situation in the Eastern Provinces. The full text of the report data is extracted as follows:

1. The mutiny of the Railway Protection Army at Manchuria Station, that is, armed resistance against Japan and opposition to the puppet Manchurian government, occupying a 260-mile zone along the railway line, put Japan in a very serious situation and made it impossible for them to rescue the Japanese advisors of the "Manchukuo" and some senior officials of the "Manchurian government." After the cavalry arrived in Manchuria, some of them were ordered to resist the Chinese Righteous Volunteer Army, but because the sorghum was everywhere, they could not move. Some of the cavalry were sent to Harbin and the area north of the Middle East Railway and its line, but due to the floods near Harbin this year, there was no progress. However, this failure of the cavalry, on the one hand, caused dissatisfaction with the cavalry among other units of the Japanese army in Manchuria, and on the other hand, it caused a great conflict between the cavalry commander and the General Headquarters of the Japanese army in Manchuria. Because the battles in various parts of Manchuria were fierce, and because its troops were distributed everywhere, the Japanese army in Manchuria showed that its army was not fully prepared for the sanitary matters of rescuing the wounded and the supply of provisions in the army, and lacked personnel to transport the wounded (especially in areas far from the railway) and treat the wounded. Therefore, many soldiers were very tired due to the above reasons and because they had been fighting for a long time, and expressed dissatisfaction with their superiors. Moreover, some Japanese troops often looted from the people because provisions could not be supplied on time, which on the one hand aroused the opposition of the people, and on the other hand, it indulged the soldiers in carrying out looting, resulting in the decline of military discipline and giving the left-leaning parties an excuse to incite in the army. Therefore, the Japanese army commander has been very uneasy recently.

Although the Japanese detectives seem to have a good organization on the surface, it is actually proven that they are not fully trained. There are only seven Japanese intelligence agencies in Harbin alone. Their work is subject to the orders of various military and administrative agencies of their headquarters, and there is no mutual contact between them. Therefore, the information they obtain often loses its timeliness. From the beginning of the Manchurian Incident until the spring of this year, the Japanese reconnaissance work in Manchuria was assisted by a large number of White Russian émigrés. The Japanese side has now abandoned the White Russian émigrés. Mr. Zhang Boling was also entrusted to go to Shandong. The military authorities all expressed that they would immediately stop the war. Regarding the Sichuan incident, Liu Xiang and Liu Wenguang also sent telegrams to the association, stating that they would never engage in internal war. However, in fact, the conflict between Sichuan and Shandong has not stopped, and it is not known how it will expand. In these two months, experience has shown that, on the one hand, it proves that the concerns of our colleagues are not excessive. Even in the midst of national crisis, there are many soldiers who still do not care. They do not pay attention to our national public opinion and are still hypocritical. On the other hand, it proves that our General Alliance to Abolish Internal War is still weak and cannot have the effect of dissuading or stopping it. The reason for this can be said to be that the association was established too recently, or that the organizers are not doing their best, but I think the root cause is that comrades like to stand outside the circle of the General Alliance to Abolish Internal War to criticize and supervise, and do not like to stand inside the circle to share responsibilities and think of ways together. Although nearly 500 groups have joined the association, it is still a small number compared to the size of China. For example, in the recent Shandong incident, only two or three groups in Jinan have joined the association, and there are no groups that have joined the association in Yantai. There are also not many individual members in both locations, so our temporary sports work has encountered various difficulties. When the General Alliance to Abolish Internal War was first launched in May, I gave a speech at Nankai University, saying that the effectiveness of the association depends entirely on the number of people who join it. Now the General Association is doing its best to urge the establishment of more branches across the country and to recruit more members in order to increase its strength. On the occasion of the establishment of the Peiping branch, I would like to report the opinions of everyone in the General Association, hoping that all members will do their best to introduce comrades, and at the same time, I hope that the national public opinion circle will cooperate and promote it in addition to criticizing and supervising, and do not think that the General Alliance to Abolish Internal War is privately owned by a small number of members who have joined it. In fact, we believe that this organization will not have great and rapid effectiveness unless it is publicly owned by the majority of the people. We believe that the movement to abolish internal war will inevitably succeed, because if it does not succeed, internal war every day is equivalent to suicide every day. In this world, China will inevitably be subjugated. In other words, if we believe that China will not be subjugated, we should believe that the movement to abolish internal war will inevitably succeed, but whether it can succeed sooner depends on the efforts of the people throughout the year. After Mr. Wu finished his report, Leng Jiaji, a member of the preparatory committee of the Peiping branch, reported on the preparatory process. Then, the branch's constitution was revised and passed. It was originally scheduled to elect five standing committee members on the spot, but due to time constraints, it was decided by public discussion to use the postal voting method. The ballots were limited to being delivered to the preparatory committee within ten days, and the ballots were opened in public. Five members of the preparatory committee were designated as members of the election committee. After the discussion, the meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

The Fifth Division Recovers the Bandit Den in Eastern Jiangxi 86

Fang Shao No Longer Has a Base in Eastern Jiangxi

The Armies of Zhejiang, Fujian, Anhui, and Jiangxi are Jointly Suppressing

Nanchang Dispatch: The military campaign to suppress the communists in Jiangxi Province is most tense in eastern Jiangxi. Therefore, since the Fifth Division of Zhou Hunyuan was transferred back to Guixi from Fuzhou, the armies have taken an offensive against the bandit troops of Fang Shao in the seven counties under the old Guangxin prefectures. Their forces include the divisions of Zhao Guantao, Li Yunheng, Ruan Zhaochang, Zhou Hunyuan, and Wang Jinwen. They have adopted a four-sided encirclement, with the destination of their convergence being Hengfeng and Geyuan. After the general attack, Fang Shao first abandoned the bandit dens in the lower reaches of the Xin River. For example, Fulin in Wannian and Zhoufang on the border between Yujiang and Guixi had already been recovered by Li's division. The bandits' puppet 10th Army and Red Police Division completely retreated to the upper reaches of the Xin River and near the Fujian-Zhejiang border. After the battle of Chepan, the bandits withdrew from the bandit dens on the south bank of the upper reaches of the Xin River and retreated to a corner on the north bank of the upper reaches of the Xin River. According to Zhou Shida, a soldier of the puppet Red Police Division who surrendered to Li's division, Fang's bandits' puppet 10th Army crossed the Xin River through Huangshagang from northern Fujian in early October and entered Geyuan, immediately ordering the soviets of various counties to order the people to rush to send straw shoes and cloth shoes for combat use. After Hengfeng County was recovered by Xiao's brigade of Zhou's division on the 10th of October, Fang Shao regarded Geyuan as the final bastion, attempting a desperate gamble, because this place had been occupied by the bandits for three or four years, and the people had been completely banditized. After Fang's bandits lost Mopan Mountain the year before last, they used this as the capital of the puppet Jiangxi-Fujian province (called Geyuan Province), sparing no effort in its management. The puppet Jiangxi-Northeast Revolutionary Committee, the puppet Fujian-Jiangxi Provincial Government, the puppet Agricultural and Industrial Bank, and the Red Army School, etc., were all available. The arsenal they operated had 500 workers and could produce tens of thousands of bullets every day, which Fang Shao entrusted with his life. It has recently been learned from Guixi that Zhou's division stationed in Hengfeng had three or four regiments. Because bandits were as numerous as hairs in the four townships, the search and suppression have not stopped. On October 14, a company of soldiers patrolled more than ten miles away from the city and discovered a team of armed bandits. A battle was immediately engaged. The bandits fled to the northeast, and Zhou's division took advantage of the victory to pursue them straight to Geyuan, where a large number of Red bandits came out to encircle them. Just as they were in a very dangerous situation, the 29th Regiment rushed to the scene and entered Geyuan, engaging in street fighting with the bandits, killing three or four hundred bandits, and seizing more than thirty guns. The remaining bandits fled in all directions, and Fang Shao's only old nest, which he had managed for many years and was deeply rooted, was occupied by Zhou's division. All kinds of puppet agencies and all equipment were destroyed. Commander Zhou has also built fortifications around the area because of its importance, forming a strong position and stationing heavy troops to prevent the Red bandits from coming again. At the moment, Fang's bandits have disintegrated and scattered across the mountainous areas of Chong'an, Pucheng, Qianshan, Guangfeng, Shangrao, Guixi, Yiyang, Hengfeng, Dechang, Leping, Wannian, and Fuliang, attempting to revive themselves. However, the troops of Qian Yuguang, Dai Yue, Zhao Guantao, and Ruan Zhaochang on the border of Fujian, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, and Anhui have contacted each other and are engaged in suppression. Although the bandits are good at fleeing, they will have no place to use their skills. (October 30-31)

Guangdong Army Attacks Jiangxi Communist Bandits from Both Sides 87

Huang's Division on the Fujian Border Coordinates with the 19th Route Army in Suppressing

Peng's Bandits in Western Jiangxi Re-Attack Chongyi but are Repelled

Guangzhou Dispatch: Since the 19th Route Army in Fujian launched a major campaign to suppress the communist bandits in Changting, the communist bandits in Jiangxi Province have gathered more than 20,000 in the Ruijin and Shicheng area, attempting a final struggle. Guangdong Province is also coordinating with the Fujian army, sending troops to block and attack them. Huang Renhuan's division stationed in Jiaoling has moved towards the Fujian border. In the future, fierce battles will be unavoidable in places such as Jiangkou in eastern Jiangxi. At present, in addition to the main force of the Jiangxi Red bandits retreating to Ruijin, Peng Dehuai's bandits in western Jiangxi are also moving towards western Jiangxi, attempting to break through the southern line and join forces with Zhu De's troops in eastern Jiangxi. Therefore, Peng's bandits have repeatedly attacked the Ganzhou and Chongyi area in recent days. After the bandit den of Dawangdong was destroyed, Chongyi has been secured. The First Division of the First Army stationed in Ganzhou is responsible for the defense, with the guard team led by Chen Dachang. The original defensive army, Wang Dao's regiment, was transferred to Shangyou. The first and second regiments were stationed on the left and right sides of Anyingqian. Recently, Peng Dehuai's bandits, in order to respond to the red flames in eastern Jiangxi, gathered the remnant bandits on the 14th and re-attacked Chongyi. Fortunately, the defensive army was prepared in advance and sent the guard team to meet the attack. At the same time, Chen Zhang's Second Independent Brigade stationed in Dayu immediately sent Li Kangxiu's First Regiment to aid, launching a fierce attack on the bandits, killing more than thirty bandits and seizing dozens of guns, and finally repelling Peng's bandits. At present, Li's regiment of Chen Zhang's Second Independent Brigade is stationed in Yangmeisi, which belongs to Chongyi. Liang Rongqiu's regiment of the brigade is stationed in Nan'an. The First Training Regiment is still stationed in Jiudushui, and Xie Xizhen's Second Training Regiment is stationed in Nankang, increasing the defense line in southern Jiangxi and coordinating with the First Army of Yu Hanmou's troops in Ganzhou City. As for the Second Division of the First Army stationed near Ganzhou City, it is also engaged in searching for the remaining bandits.

Debate in British Tennis Circles Over Net-Cord Shots

Most Do Not Support Changing the Rules

Awaiting Opinions of Famous Players

(Reuters London Dispatch) The Advisory Committee of the International Lawn Tennis Federation's suggestion that all net-cord shots be replayed has become the center of heated debate here. Most do not support the change.

The expressed intentions of famous players participating in recent major competitions seem to be divided on this issue. However, if it were put to a vote, the majority would not support this rule change.

New Rules Will Affect the Game

If these new rules were adopted, the result would be a slowdown in the game, which is unacceptable. It would be unfair for players to be penalized for low shots that their opponents fail to reach. The current rules are naturally flawed and unjust. How this newly proposed change will be viewed is of great interest and deserves attention.

Net-Cord Shots Involve Skill

Net-cord shots are naturally more fortunate than anything else, but proponents argue that they actually involve considerable skill. A player naturally tries to hit the ball over the net as close to the tape as possible. If a player is lucky enough to have their ball graze the net and drop over, it is merely the "bad luck" of the opponent. Net-cord shots often decide the outcome of games, both big and small, and often surprise the audience.

The British Lawn Tennis Association has distributed this issue to Davis Cup players and famous clubs. The outcome is eagerly awaited by all those passionate about lawn tennis.

New Basketball Skills (20) (5)

(Not Allowed) to Reprint

Original by Claire Burcky

Translated by Zhang Guoxun and Qian Yiqin

Each teammate should quickly prepare to attack and act on time, which are the two most important conditions when throwing out-of-bounds balls. This article shows how to block the opponent's defensive players.

Player No. 4 stands outside the opponent's defensive zone and throws the ball inbounds. Player No. 3 and Player No. 5 stand near the sideline, within two or three yards. When Signal One is given, Player No. 5 immediately steps forward to block Player No. 3's guard. Player No. 3 takes advantage of the situation, receives the pass from Player No. 4, and goes straight down the line. Player No. 3's guard is blocked by Player No. 5 and Player No. 5's guard, so Player No. 3 can safely dribble the ball into the empty area and shoot.
