Free Talk

Many Sons From One Stem

Zhan Lu

It is not surprising that emperors with polygamous tendencies often had dozens of sons. Hongwu Emperor of the Ming Dynasty and Kangxi Emperor of the Qing Dynasty each had dozens of sons, although not all from the same mother.

It is more unusual to have many sons all born from the same mother. During the Kangxi era, there was a scholar's wife named Zheng who gave birth to thirty-six sons. More recently, a Mrs. Maryce in England had 169 descendants.

During the Kangxi era, a scholar named Zheng, who served as a prefectural magistrate in Jiangnan, always wore tattered clothing to court each day. The governor, recognizing his competence, generously rewarded him. Yet, his clothes remained as worn as ever. The governor suspected him of feigning poverty and questioned him. Zheng replied that he had thirty-six sons and a heavy family burden, leading to his inability to afford proper clothing and food. The governor chuckled, "You have taken too many concubines." Zheng responded, "I only have one wife. Since marrying at eighteen, she has given birth every year, each time to twins. Now, at thirty-six, I have thirty-six sons." The governor ordered them to be brought in for inspection. Zheng led his thirty-six sons into the hall, the older ones carrying the younger, the middle ones leading the youngest, quickly filling the space. The governor laughed heartily and provided Zheng with a generous allowance for his family. He also reported the matter to his superiors, who provided additional subsidies. This account is recorded in the *Jian Gu Ji*.

A Western newspaper reported that a Mrs. Maryce in Stoke-on-Trent, England, is ninety-eight years old. On the day of her birthday celebration, her descendants came to offer blessings: fourteen children, fifty-five grandchildren, ninety-nine great-grandchildren, and one great-great-grandchild, totaling one hundred and sixty-nine people, all descended from her. One from China, one from the West, one ancient, one modern—both women are worthy of endless astonishment.

If every woman were like these two matriarchs, where would we place so many little citizens on Earth? Unless the Earth could also become pregnant and give birth to hundreds of new Earths, it would be impossible.

Earthworm and Leather Ball

Zhu Jun

Two Painful Metaphors

Some say that the Chinese people are like an earthworm. If someone pierces it with a needle, it immediately contracts its body, making a brief struggle—but not resistance. When the child's conscience dawns and the needle is removed, the earthworm immediately forgets the pain the needle inflicted and returns to its original state, even though the needle scar still causes slight pain. When the child's needle visits it a second time, it again contracts its body, enduring the pain and making another struggle. However, as soon as the needle leaves its body, it immediately forgets all the suffering and reveals its original state. Piercing and contracting, contracting and piercing, the child finds it very amusing, while the earthworm being harmed considers it a normal occurrence, not worthy of shame. But if the mischievous child never realizes the cruelty of his actions and continues to pierce and pull, pull and pierce, then the earthworm's body will develop a numbness and feel no pain. The result, needless to say, will be a meek and compliant death in the child's hands.

Others say that the Chinese people are like a leather ball. At first, it is filled with plenty of air. If someone hits it, it will jump up violently, demonstrating the strength of its vitality. The harder it is hit, the higher it jumps. But if, after too much trampling, it loses its air, it will lie listlessly on the ground, no longer reacting, even if you hit it hard. Then, people can confidently cut it open and use it to patch shoes.

Of course, I am unwilling to believe these two painful metaphors, but the facts clearly confirm them. What else can I say?

Brother-in-Law

Zhong Yan

An Anecdote from the Jiaodong War

Northern soldiers are often from Caozhou, Shandong. When angry, they curse by calling someone "jiuzi" or "xiaojiuzi," much like the more common "tama de" [your mother's]. "Jiuzi" means "younger brother of the wife," the counterpart to "brother-in-law."

At the beginning of the Jiaodong War, a Liu Zhennian army officer stationed in Fushan was walking along the road with a bicycle when a villager accidentally bumped into him. Enraged, the officer wanted to slap the villager, who became terrified and repeatedly called him "brother-in-law." The officer, surprised, asked why. The villager replied, "Even if I don't call you brother-in-law, you will still call me 'jiuzi.'" By this time, a crowd had gathered. The officer flushed with embarrassment and left. This is just one humorous anecdote from the midst of the intense Jiaodong War.

Biting on Vegetable Roots

Rong Yu

"If you can bite on vegetable roots, you can do anything."

Mr. Feng Huanzhang, who has retired from public life, wears coarse cloth and chews on hard bread. How frugal! Yet, many people criticize him for being affected. I think that even if the old gentleman is hypocritical and out of step with the times, in this extravagant society, his refusal to wear imported goods and his willingness to "set an example" are admirable.

In the city, one cannot show off their wealth without extravagant eating. Spending a hundred gold coins on a meal is common and unremarkable. Therefore, someone said, "A rich family's feast is a poor man's half-year's worth of grain." This is not an exaggeration at all.

When it comes to eating, the principle is simply to avoid hunger and replenish energy. Satisfying your appetite is impossible. The ancients had a saying, "Food and sex are human nature." A single man hopes to take a wife. Once he has a plain wife, he hopes for a beautiful woman. Eating is the same. Having vegetables, he wants fish and meat. After fish and meat, he wants delicacies from land and sea. With such insatiable greed, it is better to bite on vegetable roots and find joy in hardship.

What are the benefits of biting on vegetable roots? According to health experts, vegetables can purify the blood and are rich in nutrients. According to religious people, eating vegetables can prevent killing and prolong life. Let's leave those two aspects aside. Plucking huge melons from the vine and digging fresh vegetables from the field—as long as they are cooked properly, their flavor is no less than that of fish and meat. Why must one eat fish and chew meat to be considered fortunate?

People in the countryside are used to biting on vegetable roots. Fish and meat rarely enter their homes unless there are important guests or it is a holiday. Yet, their bodies are so strong, their complexions so full of color. This shows the effectiveness of biting on vegetable roots. People in the city! I advise you to bite on vegetable roots! In the end, they taste much better than tree roots.

I remember a few lines of poetry: "Cook tofu, gourds, eggplant, and leaves." "Turnips are fat when the wine is ripe." There is pleasure in biting on vegetable roots. You can see it from these two lines of poetry. "If you can bite on vegetable roots, you can do anything." Although it is an exhortation from a moralistic teacher, we might as well try it.

The Life Philosophy of a Teacher

Sleeping Lotus

Derived From Experience

Having exhausted much effort and visited many friends, you have finally managed to find a place to eat. Now you should be planning how to keep this golden rice bowl and not lose it! Here are a few tips, please see:

(1) Towards the Principal

When you first enter the school, the principal will of course talk to you about his educational policy, you just have to listen carefully. If he asks about the content of the school you used to work at, then you must not reveal everything, and avoid mentioning economic aspects.

(2) Towards Colleagues

You should not stir up trouble by promoting new educational methods, societies, etc., although these things are welcomed by the principal, but the colleagues will suffer, and it is inevitable that you will incur resentment from your colleagues.

(3) Towards Students

When talking to students, quote more foreign leaders, then the students will look at your belly very mysteriously.

(4) Others

When you talk to others (preferably students' parents), you should speak with a flowery tongue and say: "Our students are very advanced, and no one will fail the

Local News

Workers at the Sanyou Factory Clash While Preventing the Transportation of Chrysanthemums

Worker Zhu Zhaoji and Others Severely Beaten and Injured

Twelve Suspects Arrested and Sent to the General Bureau for Disposition

The labor dispute at the Sanyou Industrial Society, though mediated by the municipal government and adjudicated by the local court, remains unresolved due to the employer's appeal. Yesterday, when the factory attempted to transport chrysanthemums, workers, upon learning of it and citing the ongoing dispute, came out to obstruct the move, leading to a clash. Details are as follows:

Obstructing the Transportation of Chrysanthemums

The Sanyou Industrial Society has a chrysanthemum garden occupying about twenty acres at the east end of the main factory in Yinxiang Township. Every autumn, during the society's big sale, the chrysanthemums grown in the garden are potted and transported to the Nanjing Road branch to be given to customers as a way to attract business. Although the factory announced its closure this year, the affiliated horticultural department has not ceased operations. Therefore, the planted chrysanthemums (estimated to be over 30,000 pots) are now in full bloom. Recently, as the autumn sale period approached, the employer intended to transport the chrysanthemums to the branch and hold a chrysanthemum exhibition before distributing them to customers. Upon hearing this, the workers, angered by the employer's defiance of government orders and refusal to pay autumn food allowances, which they saw as a deliberate attempt to prolong the dispute, resolved to prevent the transportation of the chrysanthemums. Fearing obstruction by the workers, the factory sent a letter to the local Fifth District, Fourth Precinct, requesting protection and assistance with the transportation.

Clash Occurs

Yesterday morning at nine o'clock, the factory hired four trucks from the China Moving Company and instructed workers, led by the main factory director, Lao Huimin, and staff member Yin Wenlong, to go to the horticultural department to transport the chrysanthemums. Upon seeing this, some workers stepped forward to explain the situation to the drivers, requesting them not to assist with the transportation. The Fifth District, Fourth Precinct, upon receiving a report, dispatched police officers and the factory police brigade to the scene to dissuade them and maintain order. At that moment, the workers dispatched by the factory suddenly seized the opportunity to break down the eastern garden gate and rushed into the garden, leading to a clash with the workers preventing the transportation of the chrysanthemums. Order was disrupted, and traffic was blocked. Police officers at the scene were unable to stop them. Seven workers, including Zhu Zhaoji, Sun Sanbao, Ji Fulin, Sun Bujun, Zhu Yinhai, Zhang Gentu, and Chen Yibiao, were wounded by axes and clubs. All suffered severe injuries to their hands, feet, and heads.

Suspects Arrested

Upon hearing the news, the factory union (Seventh District Cotton Weaving Industry Union) dispatched two supervisors, Zhang Yihai and Fan Bangyong, to the Fifth District, Fourth Precinct, to negotiate and request the arrest of the assailants. The Municipal Public Security Bureau also received a report and dispatched Inspector Zhen Yang to the scene. The precinct chief ordered the arrest of the suspects, including Luo Shizhong, Yang Changlin, Xu Daluo, Lin Xianshou, Hong Meishuo, Niu Jinye, Luo Shixuan, Luo Ailin, Hong Daoyun, Yang Mingfa, Luo Shengfu, Zhang Huagui, and twelve others. Considering the gravity of the case, the precinct chief interrogated them before sending the suspects and injured workers to the General Bureau for further investigation.

Party and Government Investigation

After the incident, the Seventh District Cotton Weaving Industry Union dispatched representatives Xia Zhongzhao and Gong Zishen to the municipal party headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau to report the incident, requesting a thorough investigation and severe punishment of the assailants. Upon receiving the report, the party and government organs dispatched Long Peiyun from the municipal party headquarters and Wang Gang from the Social Affairs Bureau to the Yinxiang Port main factory to investigate the details of the dispute for further action.

Japanese Counselor Areno Speaks

Denies Opinion Paper Transported to Shanghai

Japanese Ambassador to Return Home Within Days

A Central News Agency reporter interviewed Japanese Minister to China, Akira Ariyoshi, yesterday at the Japanese Consulate General in Shanghai. First Secretary Areno appeared on his behalf. A record of the conversation is below:

Regarding Opinions on the Report

Reports from Tokyo stated that three boxes of Japan's opinions on the League of Nations investigation report had been transported to Shanghai via the Nagasaki Maru to be delivered to the Chinese government by the Japanese Ambassador. This news is completely unfounded. The embassy has not received the so-called three boxes of opinions. Even if Japan were to send opinions to China, there would certainly not be three boxes. Japan's opinions on the report will be formally announced by the Japanese government. The Japanese side has mixed reactions to the various items listed in the investigation report, supporting those beneficial to Japan and opposing those that are not, which is the same as the Chinese authorities' views on the report.

Problem of Road Construction Beyond Boundaries

When the reporter inquired about the reasons for the Japanese community's opposition to the recovery of roads constructed beyond boundaries, Areno initially stated that road construction beyond boundaries was a local issue and he did not wish to express any opinion. He then said that the Japanese community opposes the recovery because it believes there is no need to change the current situation. As for the attitude of the Japanese Embassy, it cannot express any opinion because it has not yet received instructions from the government.

Crackdown on Patriotic Movements

Areno criticized our people's patriotic movements, saying that it is not an action that civilized countries should have. He added that the actions of groups like the Blood Oath to Eliminate Traitors were worrying. Therefore, the Japanese consulate has requested Mayor Wu to crack down on them. Fortunately, these actions have gradually decreased recently. The reporter retorted, "Should civilized countries not have popular patriotic movements?" Areno casually replied, "Yes, yes."

Ariyoshi to Return Home Soon

Areno also told the reporter that Japanese Ambassador Akira Ariyoshi is scheduled to return home within days and will return to Shanghai in three weeks. All embassy affairs will be handled by Counselor Horiuchi.

Embassy Virtually Moving South

The rumor of the Japanese Embassy moving south was once rampant last year. Areno indicated yesterday that the Japanese Embassy has no intention of moving south at present. However, with almost all embassy personnel in Shanghai, it is virtually moving south. He also said that if the move were official, it would be even more convenient.

Brief News from Japan

Japanese Navy to Arrive

The Japanese Navy Ministry, on the pretext of transferring Shanghai marines from the Sasebo naval group, has dispatched a battalion of marines, totaling 500 men, to Shanghai aboard the special service ship Muroto. News was received yesterday that the naval battalion is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai this Sunday. After arriving in Shanghai, a portion will be sent to Hankou. In addition, the naval mine officers and soldiers sent to Shanghai by the Japanese Navy Ministry during the January 28th Incident will be reduced by 30, with 70 remaining, stationed in Shanghai and Hankou.

Japanese Pass Through Shanghai

During the winter in Shanghai, Japanese merchants who operate sugar businesses in the South Sea Islands returned to Japan, taking 110 Japanese laborers to Okinawa and other places to work in Japanese-owned sugar factories in Java and other places, in order to develop the Japanese presence in the South Seas. Unexpectedly, this year, Java's sugar production was excessive, and due to China's increase in import duties, very little was shipped, causing many factories to shut down. The Japanese expatriates were unable to support themselves and had to be sent back to Japan. Led by Japanese man Tatsuno, they first took a Japanese ship to Shanghai and then transferred to the Rokko Maru to return to their home country.

Robbers Rob Yuxianglong Hardware Store

Steal Bookkeeping Records and Contracts for Ransom

Has Been Robbed Three Times

Huadong News Agency reports: At 7:15 yesterday morning, when the clerk of Yuxianglong Hardware Wholesale Store at No. 4 Yideli, Zilai Street, French Concession, opened the door, five robbers suddenly arrived, taking out black long handguns and ordering them not to make a sound. Three robbers were wearing blue long gowns and bird-hunting hats, and two robbers were wearing black short shirts and pants, speaking with a local accent, claiming that they had lost more than 20,000 yuan in business and had come to borrow 2,000 yuan. After speaking, they forced eight employees into the storeroom, with one robber guarding the door. Two robbers immediately went upstairs. At that time, the store manager, Tian Hexiang, was still asleep in the bedroom. The robbers knocked on the door. The manager initially did not suspect anything and opened the door. The robber immediately pointed the gun at Tian's chest, ordering him not to make a sound. Tian's wife, daughter, and maid were also dumbfounded. The robbers forced them into the storeroom downstairs and then went upstairs to search for money and belongings. At around 8:00, they took two leather suitcases downstairs with all the robbers and put the store's account books, checks, contracts, etc. into the suitcase and fled. Before leaving, they claimed that 20 yuan could redeem it. According to the store manager, Tian, the five robbers today intended to kidnap people, but because the store clerks resembled workers, they only robbed more than 700 yuan in cash. Because the amount robbed was too small, they grabbed the contract account books, stamps, checks, and personal share certificates worth about 30,000 yuan. He has now ordered the clerks to stop payment to various stores and banks. He also said that the store was truly unfortunate. It was previously located in Xingkangli, Laomenmen, and was also patronized by robbers. After moving to this location, it was also robbed in less than half a year, but the loss was only more than 200 yuan. Unexpectedly, in less than two months, it was patronized by robbers again.

Public Security Bureau Prohibits Collection of Petty Rents

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau issued a notice: The owners and managers of real estate in this city, as well as old tenants, often privately collect petty rents from tenants or subtenants in addition to the regular rent, which is akin to extortion and violates regulations. The Municipal Government has repeatedly issued notices strictly prohibiting this, and orders have been issued to investigate and ban it. However, as time goes on, this habit is revived. It is now heard that landlords are still violating the ban and privately collecting the above-mentioned fees. This kind of harsh levy and layered exploitation is harmful to merchants and residents. In addition to issuing another notice to all district offices to earnestly investigate and ban it at any time, this notice is hereby issued, and all landlords, etc., must comply and eradicate this bad habit. If there is any further extortion, once verified, it will be investigated and dealt with severely according to the law and will not be tolerated.

Fang Canwen Accuses Uncle of Seizing Inheritance

Adopted Son Had Been Expelled Earlier

Plaintiff Has No Connection with the Fang Family

Fang Wencan, also known as Laohu, was adopted as a child by Fang Lunkui (also known as Fang Changhua), a resident of Fang's house on Chengdu Road West, Chongqing Road. As he grew up, he did not engage in proper business and often engaged in vulgar activities, so he was expelled early. Later, Lunkui's father, Fang Yaomao, passed away one after another. He did not participate in mourning or observing mourning etiquette. He wandered outside all year round. Lunkui's brother Bingkui also died many years ago. Now only one younger brother, Xikui, still lives in Fang's house. Wencan often asked his uncle Xikui for relief when he had difficulty making a living. On August 27th of this year, Xikui gave him 30 yuan at one time because he could not bear the harassment. Wencan issued a permanent entanglement note and stated in the note that he would no longer use the Fang family name. However, before the ink was dry, he relapsed and hired lawyer Lin Huanqing to file a lawsuit with the First Special District Court, accusing Fang Xikui of seizing the inheritance without providing an analysis. The lawsuit stated that his grandfather Fang Yaomao had three sons, the eldest was Zhankui, the second was Lunkui, and the youngest was the defendant. The movable and immovable property left by the grandfather was about 80,000, all in the hands of the defendant. The plaintiff is Lunkui's adopted son and should have the right to inherit the property. Please order the defendant to hand over all the property for a three-way distribution, and the plaintiff should receive 27,000, etc. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhou summoned him for trial. According to the plaintiff, he was not in Shanghai when his grandfather and parents died, so he did not know. It was found that the immovable property left behind was five rooms of Fang's house and six bungalows. As for the movable property, it was impossible to find out, etc. The defendant Fang Xikui was not present and extended lawyer Hong Shihuo to represent him in court. He stated that all the family property was divided equally by the defendant's father in the 32nd year of the Guangxu reign and a division book was drawn up. Furthermore, the defendant's eldest brother was named Bingkui, not Zhankui. The plaintiff was still unaware of the name and falsely claimed that the divided family property was not divided, but the plaintiff had been expelled by Lunkui early on and his adoptive son relationship was severed. He had no right to claim a share of the property. He also presented the division book, Yao Mao's deathbed will, and the recent self-written notes to prove that the plaintiff had nothing to do with the Fang family. The two lawyers then debated each other, and Judge Zhou ordered a judgment to be scheduled.

On the one hand, the Review Committee Wang Yiting, Xie Gongzhan, Tong Yamin, Fan Shangyan, and other 11 people were hired to form a Review Committee to review the exhibits and reward them separately. The venue was designed and arranged, and a chrysanthemum house was built in the planned scenic garden, with a chrysanthemum mountain in the middle, where precious chrysanthemum varieties were placed to avoid wind and rain and facilitate appreciation. The chrysanthemum ridges around the house are square and varied, and different kinds of famous flowers are dotted among them. At the entrance of the main road, potted chrysanthemums are arranged to form the ten characters of the 3rd Shanghai Chrysanthemum Exhibition. At the entrance, there is also a chrysanthemum tower, which stands tall and is inlaid with different-colored chrysanthemums, showing the four characters of "The World is for All" to awaken the eyes and ears of tourists. What is even more surprising is that the garden originally belonged to the plain and barren area, but now the mountains and hills undulate, the chrysanthemum ridges stretch, the springs flow in twists and turns, and the flower shadows are varied, creating a momentum to protect the chrysanthemum house. Being in it, one almost mistakenly thinks that they have entered a peach source. Therefore, before the meeting, there were already many visitors.

Ministry of Industry Strictly Prohibits Slaughtering Pregnant Ewes

The Ministry of Industry, in order to protect the permanent interests of herders due to the increasing number of exported lambskins, ordered the construction departments and social bureaus of various provinces and cities to strictly prohibit the slaughter of pregnant sheep and advised the Ministry of Finance to strictly prohibit exports. The original order is recorded as follows: As an order to comply, it has recently been found that the country's sheep herding households often slaughter pregnant ewes in winter or early spring in order to seize current petty profits. The purpose is not the ewe's skin, but to obtain the fetal lamb, because the price of this immature lambskin, or fetal lambskin, is about four times the price of the ewe's skin. For this reason, a large number of pregnant ewes are killed every season. If these ewes are not killed, each one can produce an average of two lambs, and when they grow up, the value of their meat will not only be double that of fetal lambskin, but the ewe can also exist at the same time. This cruel and uneconomical slaughter has become more and more intense recently. If it is still allowed to do so, not only will the output of adult sheepskins decrease day by day, but also sheep will be in danger of extinction. Moreover, mutton is one of the most important foods for Chinese people's daily life. As for the various items made of fetal lambskin, they are only used for decoration by a small number of wealthy people, and the consumption to satisfy the vanity of a small number of people has a great impact on the people of the whole country, which is not worth it. All the production locations and export quantities of the fetal lambskins have been ordered by the Ministry to be investigated and reported by the Tianjin Commodity Inspection Bureau. Last year, more than 700,000 pieces were exported from Tianjin alone, mostly from sheep-producing areas in the northwest and Shanxi, Hebei, Henan, and Shandong provinces. In order to protect sheep and maintain the permanent interests of herders, the Ministry should strictly ban this cruel slaughter. On the one hand, exports are prohibited to cut off sales, and on the other hand, herders are advised not to slaughter again to avoid losses. Both parties proceed, so that it can be completely prohibited. In addition to advising the Ministry of Finance to transfer orders to customs offices in North China and tax authorities to strictly investigate and prohibit the fetal lambskins and their manufactured products, and separately ordering the Tianjin and Qingdao Commodity Inspection Bureaus of the Ministry not to inspect or prohibit exports, the Ministry will issue an order to the department to comply and transfer orders to all counties under its jurisdiction, announce strict bans on the slaughter of fetal sheep, and send personnel to conduct on-the-spot advice to herders, informing them of the advantages and disadvantages, and reporting the compliance situation for future reference.

Disaster Area Fire Insurance Indemnity Association Sends Letter to the Public Works Bureau Requesting that Foreign Merchants be Advised

Issuing Public Bonds to Increase Premiums

The Company Bears No Loss, Policyholders Share the Burden

The Shanghai Fire Insurance Indemnity Association, because foreign merchant fire insurance companies have not expressed their intention to handle public bonds in the same way as Chinese merchants, sent a letter to the Public Works Bureau yesterday requesting that it inform the Foreign Merchant Association to express its intention as soon as possible to avoid further disputes. The original letter is as follows: The dispute over fire insurance indemnity in the disaster area has lasted for more than half a year, and the impact on society has been noted by Chinese and foreign authorities. The previous tens of thousands of policyholders who formed a team to claim compensation have become a serious security issue. Fortunately, the patrol officers of your bureau have a deep understanding of the righteousness and are well aware of the plight of the policyholders. The team claims for compensation, which originally came from an unavoidable act, so they do not interfere arbitrarily, so as to avoid all kinds of misfortunes. The Association is also deeply grateful. However, in the face of the serious situation of the dispute, our government also believes that there should be a considerable solution, so it instructed the Social Affairs Bureau to effectively handle it. The Social Affairs Bureau then instructed the Insurance Association to discuss a concrete plan and report it for approval, and notified the Association to advise policyholders to suspend claims and wait for a solution. The instructions from the Social Affairs Bureau stated that the only way to resolve the dispute over fire insurance indemnity in the disaster area is to issue public bonds. Chinese insurance companies have now passed the principle of issuing public bonds at the members' meeting, but there has been no expression from the foreign merchants. The Association is deeply sorry to learn about it. After all, in the same commercial port and the same business, it should be unified, so that the credit of the commercial port will not be flawed. Moreover, although the funds for the principle of issuing public bonds are raised from the increase in premiums by Chinese and foreign insurance industries, they are actually used for policyholders, and they are still taken from policyholders. The insurance companies themselves have no donations, but they only spend a lot of effort. Moreover, by issuing public bonds to resolve this major dispute, the credibility of the insurance companies in the community and the feelings of the people can be infinitely increased. Therefore, the Association believes that this method is beneficial and harmless to the insurance industry. If this opportunity is missed and no solution is found, the Association's tens of thousands of disaster-stricken policyholders will inevitably restart disputes and take extreme measures. It is difficult to predict what extent it will reach in the future. From the perspective of the disaster victims, it is unbearably pitiful, and it is also difficult for the patrol officers of your bureau to deal with. The Association, in order to prepare for a rainy day, has to sincerely inform you, and especially asks your bureau to advise the foreign merchant fire insurance association to express its intention to handle the business in the same way as the Chinese merchant as soon as possible, so that there will be no more disturbances, and the local area will be fortunate.

Buying a Car Using a Forged Bank Draft

Ni Renqing Buys a Car and Frauds

Transfers a Check, Alters it, and Cashes it Out

Ni Renqing, a 54-year-old Shaoxing native residing at No. 7 Zhaoqing Lane, North Chengdu Road, Public Concession, claimed to the Xintong Automobile Company at No. 1 Albert Road, French Concession, last month that he wanted to buy a Chevrolet car. The agreed price was 3,000 taels. Ni immediately took out a forged bank draft for 500 taels, dated October 12th, and asked the car dealership to make change for 500 taels. The car dealership owner saw that Ni was generous and had a broad face, so he believed it to be true and signed a check for 500 taels to Dao-I Bank, dated October 16th. The date of the check differed from the date of the bank draft by four days. Unexpectedly, after Ni took back the check, he erased the "ten" on the 16th and changed it to "six," and then went to the bank to withdraw 500 taels for spending. When Xintong Automobile Company went to collect the money at maturity, they realized that it was a forgery and found that the 500 taels of checks they had issued had been defrauded. They reported it to the police station and sent investigator Yang Yilong to arrest Ni. He was escorted to the Second Special Court Criminal Division yesterday. The police station lawyer Yuan Jiaohuang said that the police station had not yet investigated the case and requested a change of date for another hearing. Judge Wu approved the request for a change of date for a continued hearing.

Municipal Public Security Bureau Revises the Resident Surety Method

Submits a Request to the Municipal Government for Review

The City's Housing Surety Method has always been based on the Regulations on Punishing Kidnappers. Since the order to abolish the Regulations on Punishing Bandits was issued in May of this year, this surety method has lost its basis. The Municipal Public Security Bureau drafted the Housing Lease Rules in September of the 17th year. Several articles required the landlord to be responsible. Because of opposition from all walks of life, the rules were ordered to be suspended. The Municipal Public Security Bureau is now aware that the surety method needs to be stipulated urgently. The proposed revision of the Draft of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau Resident Surety Method is hereby submitted to the Municipal Government for review. The revision draft is as follows: (2) In order to eliminate bandits and maintain public security in this city, all residents of this city must seek proper security in accordance with the provisions of this method. (2) The resident surety method is as follows: 1. Store surety (those who have opened a store in the city for more than one year); 2. Resident surety (those who have lived in the city for more than one year and have a legitimate occupation; 3. Those who live in self-owned houses should submit the deed for inspection, or be certified by the map director and land protection officer, and be allowed to waive the surety, but those who are willing to follow the first and second items are allowed to listen; 4. Shanty towns and earthen houses should have a joint guarantee of five neighboring households; 5. Foreigners who have no guarantee may be certified by the consul in charge. If there is no treaty country, one overseas Chinese registered in the bureau guarantees it; 6. Party members and civil servants may be certified by the agency in charge and allowed to waive the guarantee; (3) The liability borne by the guarantor in the preceding paragraph is limited to harboring bandits and endangering public security; (4) When the landlord transfers the house to a tenant or subtenant (ie, second landlord, third tenant), regardless of whether it is a shop or a household, it should follow the provisions of Article 2 and order the tenant to seek security separately, or the landlord and subtenant will jointly guarantee and submit the guarantee certificate to the district office for filing; (5) If the guarantor has any changes in the place of guarantee or closes down, the guaranteed person should declare to the district office in charge and seek another guarantee; (6) If the guarantor does not want to guarantee the guaranteed person, he may declare to the district office in charge to withdraw the guarantee, and the district office in charge should order the guaranteed person to seek another guarantee at any time; (8) If the landlord or subtenant and transferor do not comply with this method, they may be punished in accordance with Article 34 of the Police Violation Law, and they will still be ordered to seek security. If there is still no security overdue, the district office in charge may report to the bureau for review; (9) If there is any unfinished matter in this method, it may be submitted for revision; (10) This method will be implemented from the date of approval by the Municipal Government.

The Tragic Case of the Chao-Shan Railway Staff Member Killed 90

The Deceased Was Chief Accountant Zhong Lanrao

The Murderer, Xie Chuan Yan, Was Arrested in Hong Kong

After Being Taken Back to Shantou, He Admitted He Killed For Money

Shantou Correspondence: Zhong Lanrao, chief of the accounting section of the Chao-Shan Railway Company, was a native of Meixian, 60 years old. He was known for his loyalty, diligence, simplicity, honesty, and gentleness, and was trusted by Zhang Rongxuan, the founder of the railway company. He had worked for the company for more than 20 years. Besides his regular office hours, Zhong would return to the company's main office at 6 PM every evening to clear accounts and count money until 7:30 PM, when he would go home for dinner. Sometimes he would return again, but it was not fixed. On the evening of October 20th, he had not returned home for dinner by 7 PM, causing his family to suspect something was wrong. At 10 PM that night, the railway police changed shifts. The guard on duty, Xu Heshang, handed over to Li Yaonan. Li inspected the doors and windows as usual to complete the handover procedure. Li noticed that the door at the back of the company, leading to the police office, was wide open. He and Xu Heshang entered the company's office to check and found bloodstains on the floor in front of the chief accountant's office, and the furniture was in disarray. They concluded that a murder had occurred. Li and Xu were horrified and ran back to the police station to report. Lanrao's son, Luchang, also an employee of the company, went to the police station because his father had not returned home for dinner. He asked the police to accompany him to search nearby. The station chief, Zhang Liang, immediately sent someone to report to the Public Security Bureau and accompanied many company employees to the board of directors to investigate. The Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched detective captain Chen Hanwen to lead a team to the scene. They found several bloodstains inside the accountant's office. The iron cabinet where the money was stored had been opened, and a company checkbook used for withdrawals from the bank and several other important accounting books were taken. 1,000 Singapore dollars in banknotes were missing, and the amount of other banknotes and cash taken was unknown. 150 silver dollars remained in the cabinet, and 250 dollars packed in a bamboo basket from the bank were still on the floor. Many silver dollars and coins were scattered on the floor and tables. On the newspaper stand outside the office, there was a heavy teak newspaper clip, two of which were broken, with the copper screws bent and blood and flesh smeared on them. Captain Chen immediately collected these items for evidence. He then searched the inside and outside of the company, and all the doors were intact, except for the surveillance room door, which was open, leading them to suspect that the murderer had escaped through this door. After repeated inspection, Chairman Lin Xinxin saw bloodstains on the water well door on the floor, with a Western-style dining knife next to it. He pried open the floor and found the body of Zhong Lanrao lying horizontally under the floor. His head was covered with a canvas bag used for holding money. When it was removed, the deceased had severe beating injuries to his brow, eyes, temples, and head. His neck and both hands were bruised and swollen. The death was extremely tragic, bringing tears to Chairman Lin's eyes. An investigation into Zhong's life revealed that he had never offended anyone. He never hesitated to advance monthly salaries or food allowances to his colleagues. He always locked his office door during office hours to prevent accidents and was always careful. This time, the murderer was able to break in and commit the crime. The deceased did not have the surveillance room key on him. How could the body be moved to the floor in that room and the hole in the floor be known unless it was premeditated? Captain Chen took the dining knife from the floor and saw that the water in the washbasins in the accounting office and surveillance room was bright red and smelled of blood, indicating that the murderer had washed himself there after committing the crime. It was clear that there were two or three accomplices. Before leaving, Captain Chen took six suspected employees, including Lin Hanming, Lin Jinzhen, Lin Xunpan, Lin Yaxing, Huang Haiqing, and Xu Heshang, to the police station for questioning. A pair of wooden clogs and a black cloth bib worn by the victim at the time were also taken away. On the 21st, the railway police station requested the court to send personnel for an autopsy. The autopsy confirmed that the deceased's injuries were caused by being beaten to death with a stick or nail. Before death, he was unable to resist or struggle. At 2 PM that afternoon, the board of directors held a meeting and decided to petition the government to arrest the murderer and bring him to justice to appease the spirit of the deceased.

Afterwards, police detectives from the Public Security Bureau learned that a strange man had moved from the Sihai Hotel to the Asia Hotel and then fled to Hong Kong the next day with a large amount of Hong Kong dollars. The hotel immediately dispatched detective Yao Bingkun to secretly investigate in Hong Kong with the help of railway company staff. They found Xie Chuan Yan and the prostitute Bi Jun, who had fled with him that day, renting a room on the sixth floor of the Emperor Hotel. The detectives immediately invited secret detectives stationed in Hong Kong to rush to the hotel to surround and arrest them. They first guarded the entrance. Two assistant detectives and one extradition committee member also arrived one after another. They entered the room to arrest them and reported to the Hong Kong government, which sent personnel to investigate. At first, they did not believe that Xie Chuan Yan had committed murder for money. However, a pair of cloth shoes stained with blood were found in Xie's luggage. With this evidence, the Hong Kong government agreed to extradition. On the 25th, the detectives escorted Xie Chuan Yan back to Shantou on the Chaozhou steamer and handed him over to the Public Security Bureau Detention Center. At 8 AM on the 26th, he was interrogated at the Detective Team Headquarters. He admitted that he had committed the murder for money at the Shantou Railway Company alone and had no accomplices. He said to just execute him by firing squad. He confessed that around 5 PM on the 20th, after the company staff had left work, only the last train from Chaozhou to Shantou remained. Because his father, Xie Liangyuan, was a major shareholder of the company, he went to the office and told the accounting section chief, Zhong Lanrao, that his father wanted to withdraw money. Zhong replied that a company note was required to do so. At the time, he needed the money urgently, so he asked where the money was hidden. Zhong replied that it was in the iron safe. He intended to open it, but Zhong locked the safe. So he picked up a newspaper clip and struck Zhong on the head three times. Zhong fainted to the ground. Fearing that Zhong would raise an alarm, he gagged him with a money bag and struck him again with the newspaper clip, accidentally hitting his eye, causing blood to gush out. He then went to the floor under the surveillance room, washed the blood off his hands, opened the safe, and took 1,000 Hong Kong dollars and about 3,000-4,000 yuan in Shantou notes. However, he lost the 1,000 Hong Kong dollars in Hong Kong, which he reported to the Hong Kong government for record. According to reports, Xie Chuan Yan's original name was Qianji, and he was from Songkou, Meixian. He was an extravagant spender and often associated with women. Because he had committed crimes in Nanyang several times, his father had hired a lawyer to publish a statement disowning him. In September, he committed another crime in Hong Kong and was deported to Shantou by the Hong Kong government. He lived in the Sihai Hotel and was deeply in love with a prostitute named Bi Fei. When his money ran out, he conceived a wicked plan. When he was taken back to Shantou, he was wearing a Western suit and showed no remorse. As for the seven employees and police officers, including Gu Wukun, who were implicated in the case and detained by the Public Security Bureau, they have now been released as they were not involved in the case (October 26).

Wuxi Barbers Stage a General Strike 96

There are more than 300 barbershops and 1,400 barbers in and outside Wuxi, mainly from Yangzhou and Zhenjiang, with barbers from Wuxi accounting for only a small number. Two years ago, they organized a trade association in accordance with regulations and established rules that were jointly observed. Last month, a new and well-equipped barber shop, Dahua Barbershop, opened on Hanchang Road and its business boomed. As a result, barbershops along the street were affected and began to compete by lowering prices. However, barbershops other than those on the street believed this would undermine the overall situation and hinder business, and they unanimously opposed it. They requested the trade association to intervene, reorganize the industry rules, and prevent barbershops on the street from freely lowering prices. The barbers also agreed with the shop owners and unanimously requested action. The trade association tried to persuade the barbershops on the street to voluntarily cancel the price reductions on the morning of the 1st to avoid harming the industry's harmony, but after half a day of efforts, there was no result. In the afternoon, the barbershops in the urban area became very angry, gathered together, and went on strike at 5 PM, intending to negotiate with the barbershops on the street that were lowering prices. However, those shops had already received the news and immediately closed their doors. That evening, a general meeting was held at the trade association, and the county party headquarters was requested to make a fair judgment. Yesterday morning, all the barbershops in the city remained closed. The county government ordered the county Public Security Bureau and its branches to send police to strictly suppress any disturbances. The county party headquarters also sent a cadre, Gao Zugao, to guide and mediate, hoping for a satisfactory resolution.

Slaughter Tax Dispute Resolved 97

In Wuxi, the slaughter tax in the urban area has always been contracted by the Meat Industry Association to the Tax Collection Office, with a quota of 226 pigs slaughtered per day. However, since last year's flood, followed by difficulties in contracting and a sluggish market, the meat industry has been particularly affected, and many have requested a reduction in the contracted quota. The newly appointed director of the Tax Collection Office, Yu Jigong, insisted on adhering to the quota. After two months of negotiations and mediation by the Chamber of Commerce, the two sides remained deadlocked. Yesterday, the Chamber of Commerce invited the county government, the education, construction, and public security bureaus, as well as the slaughterhouse, tax collection office, county treasury, and representatives of the meat industry, to conduct a final mediation. After lengthy negotiations, all parties reached an understanding and a decision was made: (1) The slaughter tax in the urban area will be temporarily calculated at 120 pigs slaughtered per day for one year, starting from the establishment of the new Tax Collection Office on September 16. The tax rate will remain at 4 jiao for the provincial education tax, 1 jiao for the county education surtax, and 5 fen for the construction special tax per pig. (2) This measure will be implemented immediately. Unpaid taxes will be paid daily before December 16. (3) Taxes before the establishment of the new Tax Collection Office on September 16, totaling three and a half months, should be negotiated by the industry after December 16 and paid in installments. The above three measures have been sent to all parties for information.

In the Chenzhangba Wang Xiaoda family robbery and arson case in the Eighth District, after the Second District Fourth Jia regiment recovered the stolen silver, it also led to the apprehension of the wanted suspect in the murder case of a post policeman of the Public Security Bureau. The main suspect, Fan Genbao, has been interrogated and executed. The accomplices in the robbery case, Chen Jinbao and Chen Peiyang, were still at large. The former day, detective captain Huang Bingzhong captured Chen Peiyang in Jinsitu Temple, Yangshupu, Shanghai, and escorted him to Chengchao on the morning of the 31st for interrogation.

Full County Wine Merchants Suspend Brewing Due to Dispute 101

All the wine merchants in the county have suspended brewing for many days due to the fact that Gao Xi, the director of the Tobacco and Alcohol Monopoly Office, increased the quota from 20,150 yuan to 27,800 yuan, which imposes excessive taxes on the distilleries. The distilleries are unable to bear the burden. The wine merchants, represented by the trade association's Zhuo Ting and Liu Daosheng, have decided to pay the taxes directly to the treasury, to counter the situation. At the same time, they jointly appealed to the central and provincial governments for assistance.

Nantong Searches for Ambushing Bandits in the Eastern Suburbs 102

Banditry has resurfaced in the eastern suburbs of Tongyi, and there are reports of Russians directing them. The central government attaches great importance to this matter and has ordered the provincial Security Department to send teams to suppress the bandits. The provincial Security Regiment Commander Zhu is leading troops in the bandit area to search for ambushing bandits to clear the source of banditry.

Recovery of Confiscated Tidal Fields 103

The provincial government has confiscated all 1,500 mu of tidal fields illegally collected by Xu Xiaoxian from the Liuhaisha tidal fields and ordered the county government to recover them from Xu. County Magistrate Zhang requested the court to bring Xu, who is currently detained in the prison of the court in another case. However, the Higher Court, according to the county court's request for instructions, ordered the county government to conduct a detailed review as the case was unclear, so as to be able to review the matter on the 1st.

Continued News of Opium Monopoly 104

The Nantong opium monopoly has become a reality. The person in charge, Wu Wenqing, came with Jiang Mingyu, an inspector from the five counties of Tong, Rugao, Chongming, Hai, and Qi, and is actively proceeding.

Resolution of the Wage Dispute of Teachers and Staff in Liuhe 105

The teachers and staff of various schools in the urban and rural areas resigned to demand their salaries, but there were no gatherings, coercion, parades, or demonstrations. However, Director Zhu Bofu falsely reported to the education department and ordered the county to arrest teachers, which caused a wave of unrest. The county district party department summoned the teachers and staff to a meeting to advise and persuade them, and followed the instructions of the provincial department to mediate and make three decisions: (1) The county party department will send a letter to the county government ordering the education bureau to announce detailed accounts within three days of receiving the letter, and at the same time send all receipts along with the list to the supervisory committee office for review, and request the provincial party department and education department to send personnel to conduct a joint liquidation. (2) For overdue salaries, a concrete plan for compensation and guarantees must be determined. (3) This week, all teachers and staff should resume their duties and attend classes as usual. The county party department will jointly inspect the situation with the county government and report it to the provincial department.

British Nationals Randomly Shoot Farmers in Pinghu 106

Farmers Fei Jinkui and his wife, Zhou, were working in the fields in Nanfuhangfang the other day, when two British employees of the Asiatic Petroleum Company, who were on vacation, brought guns to hunt. They fired a shot in the fields for no reason, hitting the Fei couple, who both fell to the ground and were in critical condition. The villagers immediately gathered around and took custody of the British nationals. The British nationals immediately took out banknotes to try to buy their freedom, but the crowd refused. They escorted the two criminals who injured the people to the county. Interrogator Qu opened the court to interrogate them. The British nationals, one named Martin and the other named Mating, admitted that they had injured people while playing around. During the confession, they also took off their rings and gave them to the interrogating official, who reprimanded them. In the midst of confusion, the interrogating official suddenly remembered the weapon and ordered it to be presented for inspection. A bailiff brought the gun, but it was not locked, and there was a bullet in the chamber. With a loud bang, the roof of the court was shattered, and splinters fell on the head of Fei Jinkui, who was already injured, leaving him unable to speak. Interrogator Qu ordered the Fei couple to be sent to the hospital and the two criminals to be detained for further investigation.

Burglary in Jinjiadou, Huzhou 107

Sun Dafu, the village head of Qiannancun in Jinjiadou, a place in the northern suburbs of this city, is a man of modest means, and he was coveted by bandits. On the night of October 30, several bandits, speaking with a Henan accent and armed with pistols and Mauser pistols, broke into his house. When Dafu heard the alarm, he opened the door and fled. His second son, Jin Fu, was unable to escape and was captured by the bandits, who beat him with iron rulers and burned him to force him to reveal where the silver was hidden. Jin Fu had no choice but to tell them, and all the silver, jewelry, clothes, and silk were stolen, resulting in a loss of nearly a thousand yuan. Jin Fu was severely injured and was taken to Wuxing Hospital in this city for treatment yesterday.

Important Education News

Ministry of Education Announces Curriculum Standards for Senior and Junior High Schools 108

Nanjing, 2nd: The Ministry of Education has formulated standards for senior high school physical education, Chinese, English, mathematics, biology, chemistry, history, music, and various other courses. Standards for junior high school physical education, health, Chinese, English, mathematics, botany, zoology, chemistry, history, manual arts, art, and children's songs, and various other courses have been announced today.

Nanjing, 2nd: The Ministry of Education issued the "Implementation Measures for Kindergarten and Elementary School Curriculum Standards" on the 1st, ordering education departments in provinces and cities to follow them.

Ministry of Education Orders Bookstores to Emphasize Leprosy in Book Compilation 109

Nanjing, 2nd: According to a request from the China Leprosy Relief Association, the Ministry of Education has issued a circular to all bookstores in the country, ordering them to pay attention to leprosy when compiling textbooks and teaching materials. It has issued a circular to the education departments of all provinces, instructing bookstores to be informed.

Chen Jianxiao Talks About Higher Education in Guangzhou 110

Sun Yat-sen University Ranks First in the Country

Financial Difficulties Make It Difficult to Implement Plans

Chen Jianxiao, the special commissioner for higher education in Guangdong appointed by the Ministry of Education, returned to Beijing last week. A reporter from the Minzu News Agency met him yesterday and inquired about the education situation in Guangzhou. Chen said that South China's culture is centered in Guangzhou, which is known for its development. However, it is located in a remote corner and is rarely noticed by the people of the country. Even Sun Yat-sen University, which was founded by Sun Yat-sen himself, was named after Sun Yat-sen after his death to commemorate him. In recent years, due to the right people in charge, its style has not changed, and its academic foundation has been greatly strengthened. In addition to the original colleges of arts, engineering, law, agriculture, and medicine, the university has also established research institutes for chemistry, economics, education, bacteriology, anatomy, physiology, pathology, and other subjects. Many professors have a spirit of research, and various facilities, such as libraries, machines, and specimens, have reached a considerable level. The colleges of agriculture and medicine are particularly large in scale. They are affiliated with agricultural fields covering about 10,000 mu, a model forest farm, a second forest farm, a first hospital, a second hospital, and a branch library of the medical college. The methods are all based on the German system, and most of the professors are also German. This is a unique feature of medical education in our country. Regarding the funding of Sun Yat-sen University, Chen also gave a detailed answer to the reporter. He said that before the 19th year of the Republic (1930), the Guangdong Finance Special Commissioner's Office allocated 140,000 yuan per month for expenses, which was barely enough. Last year, due to the plan to add departments of civil engineering and industrial chemistry and increase the salaries of professors, it was specially approved that the Ministry of Finance would allocate an additional 45,000 yuan per month for recurring expenses starting in September of the 20th year of the Republic (1931). Also, for the construction of the school buildings of the College of Agriculture, which requires approximately 886,000 yuan of national currency, it was also approved by the National Government that 30,000 yuan would be allocated by the central government per month, until it was fully allocated. The above two sums totaled 75,000 yuan per month, but since last year, only 228,000 yuan has actually been received, which has caused considerable difficulties. In addition, the university previously spent a great deal of money on purchasing books and instruments from abroad, due to the high price of gold. The students had to pay more fees due to the difficult social economy, and other administrative expenses were reduced. Therefore, it is difficult to implement all the proactive plans. As for the content, personnel, and administration of the university, Chen also briefly mentioned a few people. In terms of the number of students, Sun Yat-sen University ranks first among the universities in the country. The university headquarters has about 1,800 students, plus the students in kindergartens, elementary schools, junior high schools, and senior high schools, there are a total of more than 4,000 students. The total number of faculty and staff is more than 500. Since President Zou arrived, many changes have been made. Three-fifths of the deans have been replaced. The director of academic affairs, the director of the library, the director of accounting, the director of general affairs, the director of registration, the director of the farm, the director of the forest farm, the director of the hospital, the director of the senior high school, and the director of the junior high school have all been changed. The secretary-general and the six or seven secretaries are all newly appointed. More other faculty and staff have left. President Zou seems to be very enthusiastic in his work and has administrative talents. He has revised various regulations and changed the professors' contracts. All power is concentrated in the president and the director of academic affairs, and these measures seem to be more convenient, but they lose the spirit of professors governing the school and will make professors not participate in school affairs except for teaching. Chen did not say that he lived in Guangzhou for ten days before and after, most of the time, in addition to giving lectures at the Provincial Education Association and various schools, he inspected Sun Yat-sen University, especially the farm and medical school, which he visited in detail each time costing him at least four or five hours. The result was very satisfactory. President Zou also handed him a letter to Minister Zhu, asking him to deliver it on his behalf, in the hope that Sun Yat-sen University would be issued the funds approved last year. This matter is of great importance to the future of Sun Yat-sen University, and he intends to urge the government to pay attention to it. In addition, there are Lingnan University, National University, Guangzhou University, Guangzhou Law School, and Xia Ge Medical School in Guangzhou, all of which are private educational institutions. Chen has visited them all. He said that each school has a long history and has been run diligently to this day. The original intentions of the founders are commendable, but the land in Guangzhou is expensive, and the cost of purchasing land and building school buildings is already high, so there is little remaining to enrich the facilities. In terms of facilities, few schools have facilities that are satisfactory. This is probably inevitable. However, Lingnan University was founded by foreigners and has a basic scale, and Xia Ge is also run by foreigners, and its buildings and equipment are quite rich. These are exceptions. Most of the students in each school are diligent in their studies, and the school spirit is becoming more and more disciplined, unlike it was a few years ago. These are all good signs. The reporter believes that Chen's remarks are very detailed and records them for those who are concerned about education in South China.

Tongji University to Establish Surveying Department 111

Nanjing, 2nd: The Ministry of Education ordered Tongji University on the 2nd to establish a higher surveying department and a public health lecture hall with an affiliated research laboratory, and ordered them to prepare quickly and establish it when the next semester begins.
